                      \AttributeTok{message=}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{,}
                      \AttributeTok{warning=}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{,}

\section*{Chunk 3: Define functions to read in short 8.3 filenames}\label{chunk-3-define-functions-to-read-in-short-8.3-filenames}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 3: Define functions to read in short 8.3 filenames}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# {-}{-}{-}TROUBLESHOOTING{-}{-}{-}}
\CommentTok{\# If getting "file does not exist" or similar errors:}
\CommentTok{\# Switch the function used to read in the file e.g., if the relevant file is being read in using read\_sav() or read\_sav\_short(), switch to read\_sav\_short() or read\_sav() respectively.}

\CommentTok{\# If that didn\textquotesingle{}t work and you\textquotesingle{}re not using Windows: }
\CommentTok{\# Either modify this code chunk for your OS (note the "if" statement at the start of each function) or manually shorten the error{-}inducing file paths.}

\CommentTok{\# {-}{-}{-}}

\CommentTok{\# Purpose of this chunk: }
\CommentTok{\# To ensure R can identify and read in all necessary files.}
\CommentTok{\# This project found me making frequent use of file paths over 260 characters in length. Out of my naivete, I didn\textquotesingle{}t realize Windows File Explorer automatically shortens such file paths by rewriting them in the 8.3 filename convention{-}{-}{-}meaning R can no longer access their standard "long name." Conversely, functions like read\_sav() automatically lengthen 8.3 filenames via functions like normalizePath(), turning the true 8.3 file path into a long name which, from R\textquotesingle{}s and (thus our) perspective, is useless.}
\CommentTok{\# This code chunk turns our long name inputs into 8.3 filenames while tricking the read\_*(){-}type functions into not turning them back.}


\CommentTok{\# Context for nerds:}
\CommentTok{\# In my Registry Editor, under Computer\textbackslash{}HKEY\_LOCAL\_MACHINE\textbackslash{}SYSTEM\textbackslash{}CurrentControlSet\textbackslash{}Control\textbackslash{}FileSystem, I had set the LongPathsEnabled value to 1 (which enables Windows to use long file paths) and the NtfsDisable8dot3NameCreation value to 2. I had also changed Group Policy to "Enable Win32 long paths".}
\CommentTok{\# But none of that mattered! Windows File Explorer lacks a longPathAware entry in its .exe file\textquotesingle{}s manifest{-}{-}so despite LongPathsEnabled=1, my file paths were still capped at 260 characters. Ergo this code chunk.}
\CommentTok{\# It\textquotesingle{}s possible that setting NtfsDisable8dot3NameCreation=0 would\textquotesingle{}ve prevented all of this code from being necessary. But I\textquotesingle{}d rather not force replicators to change their registry settings.}

\CommentTok{\# {-}{-}{-}}

\CommentTok{\# Goal: Make an alternative read\_sav() which accepts 8.3 filenames}

\NormalTok{read\_sav\_short }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(long\_path, ...) \{}
  
  \CommentTok{\# shell() only exists in Windows; so if not running on Windows, just use read\_sav() normally}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{Sys.info}\NormalTok{()[}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}sysname\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{] }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \StringTok{"Windows"}\NormalTok{)\{}
    \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{read\_sav}\NormalTok{(long\_path, ...))}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Get the 8.3 alias of the file\textquotesingle{}s absolute path from shell}
\NormalTok{  short\_path }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{shell}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}for \%\%I in ("\%s") do @echo \%\%\textasciitilde{}sI\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, long\_path), }
    \AttributeTok{intern =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{    ) }\CommentTok{\# Note: Use double percent signs (\%\%) to prevent CMD shell from thinking each percent sign is a delimiter for a variable name.}
 
  \CommentTok{\# Open a connection ("con") in binary mode ("rb" = "read binary"; SPSS files are binary i.e. non{-}text files, and thus best read in as such) to the 8.3 filename}
\NormalTok{  con }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{file}\NormalTok{(short\_path, }\StringTok{"rb"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Save space by closing the connection when this function finishes executing}
  \FunctionTok{on.exit}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{close}\NormalTok{(con))}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Pass this open connection to read\_sav() so it doesn\textquotesingle{}t convert the 8.3 filename back into the long filename}
\NormalTok{  data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_sav}\NormalTok{(con, ...)}
  \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(data)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# There\textquotesingle{}s something weird happening here. In my File Explorer, the entire absolute path is not an 8.3 alias: only the relative path (the path from the working directory, or here, the names of the file and the folder containing it) is. Yet this code only works because it feeds a connection, opened via file() using an absolute path\textquotesingle{}s 8.3 alias, directly into read\_sav(). This should *automatically happen in read\_sav() anyways*!!! read\_sav(path) calls datasource(path) calls readr:::standardise\_path(path) (an internal function, see ?\textasciigrave{}:::\textasciigrave{} and https://github.com/tidyverse/readr/blob/96ddac314b47402bc63e1f81c149c463cf58e3da/R/source.R\#L119) calls readr:::detect\_compression(path) calls readBin(path) calls file(path, "rb") when \textquotesingle{}path\textquotesingle{} is a string e.g., when \textquotesingle{}path\textquotesingle{} is a file path instead of a connection. This file(..., "rb") call is exactly what happens to \textquotesingle{}con\textquotesingle{} in read\_sav\_short()! Yet it is precisely at file(..., "rb") where read\_sav() fails when called on an 8.3 file path! This is true when the whole absolute path is 8.3 (as in read\_sav\_short()) or when only the relative path is (as in my File Explorer).}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# {-}{-}{-}}

\CommentTok{\# Goal: Likewise, now for reading in CSV files}

\NormalTok{read\_csv\_short }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(long\_path, ...)\{}
  
  \CommentTok{\# shell() only exists in Windows}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{Sys.info}\NormalTok{()[}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}sysname\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{] }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \StringTok{"Windows"}\NormalTok{)\{}
    \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(long\_path, ...))}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
\NormalTok{  short\_path }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{shell}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}for \%\%I in ("\%s") do @echo \%\%\textasciitilde{}sI\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, long\_path),}
    \AttributeTok{intern =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{  )}
  
\NormalTok{  con }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{file}\NormalTok{(short\_path, }\StringTok{"rb"}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# CSVs are text, not binary, files. But read\_csv() feeds its inputs into vroom() (https://github.com/tidyverse/readr/blob/96ddac314b47402bc63e1f81c149c463cf58e3da/R/read\_delim.R\#L253), which apparently can only read from a binary connection? Otherwise vroom() calls vroom\_() (https://github.com/tidyverse/vroom/blob/73c90c4fe490c0588b20ac527c40fcb1c683683e/src/vroom.cc) which in turn calls a function which looks very similar to the source code of readBin() (https://github.com/SurajGupta/r{-}source/blob/a28e609e72ed7c47f6ddfbb86c85279a0750f0b7/src/library/base/R/connections.R\#L219). The vroom package seems to only call readBin() at vroom:::R\_ReadConnection() (https://github.com/tidyverse/vroom/blob/73c90c4fe490c0588b20ac527c40fcb1c683683e/src/connection.h\#L52), though I\textquotesingle{}m not sure how the call chain could go from vroom\_() to R\_ReadConnection(){-}{-}nor am I sure as to why read\_csv() reads in text files as binary. Perhaps read\_csv() reads in the raw bytes using readBin() before applying its own parser to the text?}
  \FunctionTok{on.exit}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{close}\NormalTok{(con))}
  
\NormalTok{  data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(con, ...)}
  \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(data)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# {-}{-}{-}}

\CommentTok{\# For Excel files}

\CommentTok{\# Note: read\_excel() only accepts file paths as strings, not connections (see https://github.com/tidyverse/readxl/blob/main/R/read\_excel.R\#L183 and https://github.com/tidyverse/readxl/blob/2a7f6efd8562ca5beba0b34933c8e4a9332ed6a8/src/Read.cpp\#L86). It seems like all similar functions are the same, too.}

\NormalTok{read\_excel\_short }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(long\_path, }\AttributeTok{sheet =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, ...)\{ }\CommentTok{\# We want sheet = 1 to be the default for all commands within this function }
  
  \CommentTok{\# shell() only exists in Windows}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{Sys.info}\NormalTok{()[}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}sysname\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{] }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \StringTok{"Windows"}\NormalTok{)\{}
    \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{read\_excel}\NormalTok{(long\_path, }\AttributeTok{sheet =}\NormalTok{ sheet, ...))}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Split long\_path into its two components: the folder and the file}
\NormalTok{  long\_folder }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{dirname}\NormalTok{(long\_path)}
\NormalTok{  long\_file }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{basename}\NormalTok{(long\_path)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Extract the 8.3 alias of the folder\textquotesingle{}s absolute path}
\NormalTok{  short\_folder }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{shell}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}for \%\%I in ("\%s") do @echo \%\%\textasciitilde{}sI\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, long\_folder), }
    \AttributeTok{intern =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{    )}
  
  \CommentTok{\# There seems to be no similar way to get the file\textquotesingle{}s 8.3 alias safely. To bypass this, we run a directory call on the folder\textquotesingle{}s 8.3 name, which lists out all the files in the folder, identified by both their long and short names.}
\NormalTok{  dir\_output }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{shell}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}dir /x "\%s"\textquotesingle{}}\NormalTok{, short\_folder),}
    \AttributeTok{intern =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{  )}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Identify the relevant file\textquotesingle{}s row as the one which includes an exact match (ergo "fixed", meaning no regex parsing) to long\_file and then store it (ergo "value"). }
\NormalTok{  candidate\_line }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(long\_file, dir\_output, }\AttributeTok{value =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{fixed =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# grep() searches through a vector of strings and returns the indices or values of elements which contain a match.}

  
  
  \CommentTok{\# To identify the file\textquotesingle{}s 8.3 name from this row, see https://tomgalvin.uk/blog/gen/2015/06/09/filenames/: a file name of 8 characters or more is upper{-}cased, stripped of its invalid characters (e.g., spaces), truncated to the first 6 characters of its basename, and then followed by a tilde, a single digit, and the first 3 characters of its upper{-}cased file extension en route to becoming an 8.3 filename.}
  
\NormalTok{  pattern }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"([A{-}Z0{-}9{-}]\{1,8\}\textasciitilde{}[0{-}9]}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{.[A{-}Z0{-}9]\{1,3\})"} \CommentTok{\# "(...)" = capturing group, though only used here for cleanliness; "[A{-}Z0{-}9]\{1,8\}" = match with 1{-}8 uppercase letters or digits; "\textasciitilde{}" = match with a tilde; "[0{-}9]" = match with exactly one digit; "\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}." = match with a period (as "\textbackslash{}" is an escape character in both R and regex, meaning "\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}." in R = "\textbackslash{}." in regex = "." in text)}
  \CommentTok{\# Note that, excluding the working directory, 8.3 filenames must be weakly less than 8 characters. Ergo "\{1,8\}"}
  
\NormalTok{  match }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{regexpr}\NormalTok{(pattern, candidate\_line, }\AttributeTok{perl =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\#regexpr() searches a single string and returns an integer vector indicating the starting position of the first match and the length of the matched text. Perl{-}style matching is used for its speed (per the regexpr() documentation) and flexibility (see https://gist.github.com/CMCDragonkai/6c933f4a7d713ef712145c5eb94a1816) over the default POSIX{-}style matching.}
  
  \CommentTok{\# I\textquotesingle{}m not entirely sure why this code is working so well; just in case, I\textquotesingle{}m including error codes for your benefit.}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (match[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] }\SpecialCharTok{==} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)\{}
    \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Could not find the file\textquotesingle{}s 8.3 alias from the folder\textquotesingle{}s directory listing."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Extract the file\textquotesingle{}s 8.3 alias from this match data}
\NormalTok{  short\_file }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{regmatches}\NormalTok{(candidate\_line, match)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Construct the absolute short path using short names}
\NormalTok{  abs\_short }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(short\_folder, short\_file)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Copy the file to a temporary one so that our file readers won’t re{-}normalize its path}
\NormalTok{  ext }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{tolower}\NormalTok{(tools}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{file\_ext}\NormalTok{(short\_file)) }\CommentTok{\# Extract the file\textquotesingle{}s extension}
\NormalTok{  temp\_file }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{tempfile}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{fileext =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"."}\NormalTok{, ext))}
  
  \CommentTok{\# In case your computer is messing up in ways mine wasn\textquotesingle{}t.}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{file.copy}\NormalTok{(abs\_short, temp\_file, }\AttributeTok{overwrite =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))\{}
    \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"File failed to copy from its short path to a temporary location."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Using read\_excel() would return an error from libxls, the C library. So we turn to other packages instead.}
  \CommentTok{\# Only use xlsx package to read in .xls to limit the need for Java}
  \CommentTok{\# Load the packages via namespace so they only need to be installed if needed. Use xlsx::read.xlsx for .xls files.}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Read in from the temporary file}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (ext }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"xls"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"xlsm"}\NormalTok{)) \{}
    
    \CommentTok{\# If needed namespace is installed, read in the file}
    \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{requireNamespace}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"xlsx"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{quietly =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)) }
      \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Install the }\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{xlsx}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{ package and Java (see https://www.java.com/en/download/manual.jsp)."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ xlsx}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{read.xlsx}\NormalTok{(temp\_file, }\AttributeTok{sheetIndex =}\NormalTok{ sheet, ...)}
\NormalTok{  \} }
  
  \CommentTok{\# Repeat}
  \ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (ext }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"xlsx"}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{requireNamespace}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"openxlsx"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{quietly =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))\{}
      \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Install the }\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{openxlsx}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{ package."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    \}}
\NormalTok{    data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ openxlsx}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{read.xlsx}\NormalTok{(temp\_file, }\AttributeTok{sheet =}\NormalTok{ sheet, ...)}
\NormalTok{  \} }
  
  \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(data)}
  
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# From the Census of India 2001}
\NormalTok{data\_folder }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"Indian Census 2001"}

\CommentTok{\# start.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# 35 files will be read in. Preallocate list to store their cleaned data}
\NormalTok{files }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list.files}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  data\_folder,}
  \AttributeTok{pattern =} \StringTok{"\^{}PC01\_C16\_}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{2\}}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{.xls$"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{full.names =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{result\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{vector}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"list"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(files))}

\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (i }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{seq\_along}\NormalTok{(files)) \{}
\NormalTok{  file\_path }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ files[i]}
\NormalTok{  temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_excel}\NormalTok{(file\_path, }\AttributeTok{skip =} \DecValTok{6}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{col\_names =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Explicitly set column names}
  \FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(temp) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"table"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"state\_code"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"district\_code"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"tehsil\_code"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"area\_name"}\NormalTok{,}
                      \StringTok{"mother\_tongue\_code"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"mother\_tongue"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"spkr\_tot"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"m\_spkr\_tot"}\NormalTok{,}
                      \StringTok{"f\_spkr\_tot"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"spkr\_urban"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"m\_spkr\_urban"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"f\_spkr\_urban"}\NormalTok{,}
                      \StringTok{"spkr\_rural"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"m\_spkr\_rural"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"f\_spkr\_rural"}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Extract the state name:}
  \CommentTok{\# Find the first row in the area\_name column that begins with "State {-} "}
\NormalTok{  state\_val }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{area\_name[}\FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}State {-} "}\NormalTok{, temp}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{area\_name)]}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(state\_val) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
\NormalTok{    state }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{NA\_character\_}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{    state }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ state\_val[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
      \CommentTok{\# Remove the "State {-} " prefix}
      \FunctionTok{str\_remove}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}State {-}}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{s*"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \CommentTok{\# Remove four{-}digit suffix code}
      \FunctionTok{str\_remove}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{s*}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{4\}$"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \CommentTok{\# Remove leading/trailing spaces. Squish internal spaces}
      \FunctionTok{str\_squish}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \CommentTok{\# Convert to title case}
      \FunctionTok{str\_to\_title}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Filter the dataframe for rows where both:}
  \CommentTok{\# 1. "mother\_tongue\_code" ends with "0"}
  \CommentTok{\# 2. "area\_name" begins with "District {-} "}
\NormalTok{  temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{str\_detect}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(mother\_tongue\_code), }\StringTok{"0$"}\NormalTok{),}
           \FunctionTok{str\_detect}\NormalTok{(area\_name, }\StringTok{"\^{}District {-} "}\NormalTok{))}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Create "district" and "state" columns}
\NormalTok{  temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
      \CommentTok{\# Create "district" by cleaning "area\_name"}
      \AttributeTok{district =}\NormalTok{ area\_name }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
        \FunctionTok{str\_remove}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}District {-}}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{s*"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
        \FunctionTok{str\_remove}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{s*}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{4\}$"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
        \FunctionTok{str\_squish}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
        \CommentTok{\# Remove all trailing non{-}letters}
        \FunctionTok{str\_replace}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"[\^{}[:alpha:]]+$"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{),}
      
      \CommentTok{\# Create "state" via extracted state name}
      \AttributeTok{state =}\NormalTok{ state}
\NormalTok{    )}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Clean "mother\_tongue" column}
\NormalTok{  temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{mother\_tongue =}\NormalTok{ mother\_tongue }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
             \FunctionTok{str\_remove}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{1,3\}}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{s+"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# Remove leading 1{-}3 digits and a space}
             \FunctionTok{str\_to\_title}\NormalTok{()) }\CommentTok{\# Title case}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Save cleaned df in list}
\NormalTok{  result\_list[[i]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Combine cleaned dfs}
\NormalTok{census01 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(result\_list)}

\CommentTok{\# end.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# end.time {-} start.time }
\CommentTok{\# For us, above order (clean files, then bind) was 1.48 secs faster than alternatives.}

\section*{Chunk 5: Match districts: Extract district info from key datasets}\label{chunk-5-match-districts-extract-district-info-from-key-datasets}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# From NSS 2007{-}08 Participation and Expenditure in Education, 64th Round}

\NormalTok{data\_folder }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"NSS 2007{-}08 Participation and Expenditure in Education 64th Round"}

\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_xlsx}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(data\_folder, }\StringTok{"DDI Metadata from Nesstar XML.xlsx"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{suppressWarnings}\NormalTok{()}

\NormalTok{districts\_only\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(name }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"district\_code"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:labl25}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{distinct}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{str\_detect}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"\^{}}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{5\}$"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# \^{} = start of string, \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}d\{5\} = exactly five digits, $ = end of string. Filters out codes which are actually for states (2 digits long) or regions (3 digits), keeping only true district codes (5 digits).}
  \FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{district\_code\_0708 =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{district\_0708 =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:labl25}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{state\_code\_0708 =} \FunctionTok{substr}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_0708, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{region\_code\_0708 =} \FunctionTok{substr}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_0708, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    )}

\NormalTok{regions\_only\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(name }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"region\_code"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:labl25}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{distinct}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{str\_detect}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"\^{}}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{3\}$"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# \^{} = start of string, \textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}d\{3\} = exactly three digits, $ = end of string. Filters for regions (3 digits).}
  \FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{region\_code\_0708 =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{region\_0708 =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:labl25}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{states\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(name }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"STATE"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:labl25}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{distinct}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:labl25}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{state\_code\_0708 =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:catValu}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{state\_0708 =} \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{ns1:labl25}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{districts\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(states\_0708, districts\_only\_0708, }\AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"state\_code\_0708"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{districts\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(districts\_0708, regions\_only\_0708, }\AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"region\_code\_0708"}\NormalTok{)}





\CommentTok{\# From NSS 2017{-}18 Household Social Consumption Education, 75th Round}
\NormalTok{data\_folder }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"NSS 2017{-}18 Household Social Consumption Education 75th Round Data July 2017 {-} June 2018"}

\CommentTok{\# Huge thanks to Tabula for helping me turn the original PDF table into a CSV!}
\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv\_short}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(data\_folder, }\StringTok{"List of Districts NSS 2017{-}18.csv"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{col\_names =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"sl. no (1)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"state\_1718"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"region\_code\_1718"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"region\_1718"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"sl. no (5)"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"district\_1718"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"district\_only\_code\_1718"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{col\_types =} \StringTok{"dcccdcc"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{districts\_1718 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(district\_1718)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{fill}\NormalTok{(region\_code\_1718, }\AttributeTok{.direction =} \StringTok{"down"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# In the original table, region\_code was only given for the first district listed within each region{-}{-}all other districts had an NA.}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{district\_only\_code\_1718 =} \FunctionTok{gsub}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"[()]"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, district\_only\_code\_1718), }\CommentTok{\# Characters enclosed by square brackets form a character class, a pattern which matches with any character also found inside of the class. So here, we globally substitute ("gsub") an empty string for any character in the district\_only\_code column which matches the class "[()]" i.e., for any "(" or ")".}
    \AttributeTok{district\_code\_1718 =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(region\_code\_1718, district\_only\_code\_1718) }\CommentTok{\# Row by row, append the newly de{-}parenthesized district\_only\_code to the end of region\_code.}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_1718, district\_1718) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{state\_code\_1718 =} \FunctionTok{substr}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_1718, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{arrange}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_1718)}

\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(data\_folder, }\StringTok{"State Codes.csv"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{col\_names =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_1718"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"state\_code\_1718"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{col\_types =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"cc"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{skip =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{districts\_1718 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{right\_join}\NormalTok{(districts\_1718, temp, }\AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"state\_code\_1718"}\NormalTok{)}


\CommentTok{\# Drop geometry. Keep JID + keys}
\NormalTok{districts\_20 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_bnds\_20 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{st\_drop\_geometry}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(JID, district\_20, state\_20)}


\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Diagnose and fix issues \#\#\#\#}

\CommentTok{\# Fix 2007{-}08 districts which are assigned multiple codes}
\CommentTok{\# Test for their presence:}
\CommentTok{\# districts\_0708 \%\textgreater{}\% group\_by(state\_0708) \%\textgreater{}\% distinct(district\_0708) \%\textgreater{}\% nrow()}
\CommentTok{\# Returns 595}
\CommentTok{\# districts\_0708 \%\textgreater{}\% group\_by(state\_0708) \%\textgreater{}\% distinct(district\_code\_0708) \%\textgreater{}\% nrow()}
\CommentTok{\# Returns 598}
\CommentTok{\# View the suspected culprits:}
\NormalTok{repeated\_districts\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ districts\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(district\_0708, state\_0708) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{summarize}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{n =} \FunctionTok{n\_distinct}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_0708)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(n }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{repeats\_of\_districts\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ districts\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  district\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ repeated\_districts\_0708}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{district\_0708,}
\NormalTok{  state\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ repeated\_districts\_0708}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{state\_0708}
\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{\# Clear the innocent suspects:}
\NormalTok{used\_repeats\_of\_districts\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ edu0708b4 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  district\_code }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ repeats\_of\_districts\_0708}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{district\_code\_0708}
\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(district\_code) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{summarize}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{())}
\CommentTok{\# Charge the true culprits}
\NormalTok{unused\_repeats\_of\_districts\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ repeats\_of\_districts\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
    \SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{district\_code\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ used\_repeats\_of\_districts\_0708}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{district\_code}
\NormalTok{  )}
\CommentTok{\# Convict them}
\NormalTok{districts\_0708 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ districts\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
  \SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{district\_code\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ unused\_repeats\_of\_districts\_0708}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{district\_code\_0708)}

\CommentTok{\# Repeat for 2017{-}18}
\CommentTok{\# \# Test for presence of guilt:}
\CommentTok{\# districts\_1718 \%\textgreater{}\% group\_by(state\_1718) \%\textgreater{}\% distinct(district\_1718) \%\textgreater{}\% nrow()}
\CommentTok{\# \# Returns 672}
\CommentTok{\# districts\_1718 \%\textgreater{}\% group\_by(state\_1718) \%\textgreater{}\% distinct(district\_code\_1718) \%\textgreater{}\% nrow()}
\CommentTok{\# \# Returns 672}
\CommentTok{\# \# All good!}
\end{Highlighting}

\section*{Chunk 6: Match districts: Construct district tracking dfs}\label{chunk-6-match-districts-construct-district-tracking-dfs}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 6: Match districts: Construct district tracking dfs}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# The districts listed in 2007{-}08 vs. 2017{-}18 vary for two reasons: legitimate political changes (districts may have been created, destroyed, or renamed) and typos. I address both here.}


\CommentTok{\# Import data on district changes}
\NormalTok{data\_folder }\OtherTok{=} \StringTok{"District Changes Data"}

\NormalTok{district\_timeseries }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_excel\_short}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(data\_folder, }\StringTok{"Time series{-} State and Districts Changes {-}Alluvial 1951{-}2024.xlsx"}\NormalTok{)) }
\CommentTok{\# Though its extensive time range is informative, there seem to be some typos and factual errors here (e.g., the 2019 merger of Dadra and Nagar Haveli with Daman and Diu is not reflected here, and "Dadra" is twice misspelled as "Dadara")}
\CommentTok{\# But not as many mistakes as my original district\_tracker, turns out! :D}

\NormalTok{years\_of\_interest }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{2001}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2011}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2024}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{district\_timeseries }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_timeseries }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# Select only XYYYY{-}State and XYYYY{-}District for those years}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{matches}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}("}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(years\_of\_interest, }\AttributeTok{collapse=}\StringTok{"|"}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{")[{-}–](State|District)$"}\NormalTok{))) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# Rename to state\_yy / district\_yy}
  \FunctionTok{rename\_with}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{tolower}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{str\_replace}\NormalTok{(.x, }\StringTok{"\^{}(?:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{2\})(}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{2\})[{-}–](State|District)$"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{2\_}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{1"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  ))}
  

\CommentTok{\#district\_creations \textless{}{-} read\_excel\_short(file.path(data\_folder, "New Districts Created between 1951{-}2024.xlsx")) \%\textgreater{}\% select(!c.............................................................) \# Some files gained an empty column upon importing}

\CommentTok{\#district\_renamings \textless{}{-} read\_excel\_short(file.path(data\_folder, "Name Changes\_Districts\_Indian States\_1951{-}2021.xlsx")) \%\textgreater{}\% select(!c.............................................................)}

\CommentTok{\#district\_splits \textless{}{-} read\_excel\_short(file.path(data\_folder, "District Splits and Carve outs{-}decadewise  1951{-}2024.xls")) \%\textgreater{}\% select(!c.............................................................)}


\CommentTok{\# {-}{-}{-}}


\CommentTok{\# Justify the district\_tracker df method of matching }

\CommentTok{\# We want to make it so that for each 2017{-}18 district, either it can be directly matched to a single 2007{-}08 district, or a single 2007{-}08 district can be matched to it. To do so, all district changes must have been either clean partitions or name changes of old districts{-}{-}new districts being carved out of multiple old districts and/or new borders being drawn between old districts make it far harder to equate or claim equality between units of analysis across time.}


\CommentTok{\# Up to 2001, @kumarCreatingLongPanels2016 are able to measure the *proportion* of each district\textquotesingle{}s population that was allocated into a new district as a result of district changes, specifically those which are not clean partitions: so carve{-}outs (of new districts from old districts), mergers, renamings, and border shifts. Carve{-}outs from multiple districts at once and border shifts are the most troublesome for us, as they prevent us from directly matching new districts to a single old district. There does not seem to be any data on how such district carve{-}outs or border shifts have allocated populations between districts since 2001.}

\NormalTok{district\_carveouts\_shifts\_9101 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv\_short}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(data\_folder, }\StringTok{"District Carve{-}Outs and Renamings 1961{-}2001.csv"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{col\_names =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"district\_1991"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"pop\_1991"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"district\_2001"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"pct\_01in91"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"pct\_91in01"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{col\_types =} \StringTok{"cccdd"}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{fill}\NormalTok{(district\_1991, pop\_1991, }\AttributeTok{.direction =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"down"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(pct\_91in01))}

\CommentTok{\# So we justify directly matching districts by showing that most district changes from 1991 to 2001 were equivalent to renamings, partitions, or mergers.}

\NormalTok{plt\_district\_carveouts\_shifts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_carveouts\_shifts\_9101 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{ggplot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x =}\NormalTok{ pct\_91in01)) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{geom\_histogram}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{binwidth =} \FunctionTok{diff}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{range}\NormalTok{(district\_carveouts\_shifts\_9101}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{pct\_91in01, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{))}\SpecialCharTok{/}\DecValTok{40}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{fill =} \StringTok{"goldenrod"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{guides}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{fill =} \StringTok{"none"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+} 
  \FunctionTok{labs}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{y =} \StringTok{"Number of 2001 Districts"}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{x =} \StringTok{"Percentage of a 1991 District\textquotesingle{}s Population in the 2001 District"}
    \CommentTok{\# title = "Population Reallocations From District Shifts and Carve{-}Outs, 1991{-}2001",}
    \CommentTok{\# subtitle = "Number of 2001 Districts Which Absorbed a Percentage of a 1991 District\textquotesingle{}s Population"}
\NormalTok{    )}
\CommentTok{\# From 1991 to 2001, it\textquotesingle{}s evident that district changes which did not involve clean partitions were rarely associated with changes in district populations. In other words, most of these changes were approximately equal to name changes. \^{}[While most of these changes were actually *precisely* name changes, some were not. See @kumarCreatingLongPanels2016, for example, to see that certain changes only involved transfers of uninhabited land.]}


\CommentTok{\# To get the exact proportion of "other" district changes which are not equivalent to renamings:}
\CommentTok{\# Check pctortion of district changes which allocated less than 100/c or 100 {-} 100/c of the old district\textquotesingle{}s population to the new district }
\NormalTok{c }\OtherTok{=} \DecValTok{40}

\NormalTok{int\_bnds }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_carveouts\_shifts\_9101 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{min =} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(pct\_91in01),}
    \AttributeTok{max =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(pct\_91in01),}
    \AttributeTok{mesh =}\NormalTok{ (max }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ min) }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ c,}
    \AttributeTok{int\_lower =}\NormalTok{ min }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ mesh,}
    \AttributeTok{int\_upper =}\NormalTok{ max }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ mesh,}
    \AttributeTok{n =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{(),}
    \AttributeTok{n\_ext =} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      pct\_91in01 }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=}\NormalTok{ min }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ mesh }\SpecialCharTok{|} 
\NormalTok{        pct\_91in01 }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ max }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ mesh),}
    \AttributeTok{pct\_ext =}\NormalTok{ n\_ext}\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{n}
\NormalTok{  )}

\CommentTok{\# (Set c = 40) 86\% of allocations from a parent district to a child district upon an "other" type of district change involved a transfer of more than 97.5\% or less than 2.5\% of the population. Meaning 86\% of the time, the new district almost precisely matched the old district{-}{-}the change was effectively a name change. }

\NormalTok{carveshift\_count }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_carveouts\_shifts\_9101 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(district\_2001) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{arrange}\NormalTok{(district\_2001) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{summarize}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{max\_pct =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(pct\_91in01),}
    \AttributeTok{min\_pct =} \FunctionTok{min}\NormalTok{(pct\_91in01),}
    \AttributeTok{num\_parents =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{carveshift =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(max\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ int\_bnds}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{int\_upper }\SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ min\_pct }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=}\NormalTok{ int\_bnds}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{int\_lower, }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}

\CommentTok{\# mean(carveshift\_count$carveshift)}
\NormalTok{pct\_ok\_annoying\_districts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{{-}} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(carveshift\_count}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{carveshift)}\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{int\_bnds}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{n}
\CommentTok{\# = 0.9335106 if c=40, so 93.4\% of district changes that were not clean partitions were equivalent to a name change (allocating more than 97.5\% or less than 2.5\% of the old district\textquotesingle{}s population).}

\CommentTok{\# We use this as justification to assume away other types of district changes (namely district carve{-}outs and border shifts), allowing us to match each new district to a single old district or vice versa. }

\CommentTok{\# This is equivalent to what @jaacksIndiaDistrictChanges2020 did in their tracking of district changes from 2001 to 2020, with the children of district carve{-}outs only matched with the one parent who contributed the most to their land area; likewise for districts following border shifts. We thus use their data below.}


\CommentTok{\# {-}{-}{-}}


\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Construct district\_tracker df \#\#\#\#}


\CommentTok{\# Import data, do preliminary data cleaning}

\NormalTok{data\_folder }\OtherTok{=} \StringTok{"District Changes Data"}
\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_ods}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{file.path}\NormalTok{(data\_folder, }\StringTok{"IndiaDistrictTracker2001to2020.ods"}\NormalTok{), }\AttributeTok{col\_names =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{temp\_names }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{tibble}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{year =} \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(temp[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,])) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{fill}\NormalTok{(year) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{pull}\NormalTok{(year)}

\FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(temp) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste}\NormalTok{(temp\_names, }\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(temp[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{,]), }\AttributeTok{sep =} \StringTok{"\_"}\NormalTok{)}


\CommentTok{\# Set column names as interleaved named vector}

\NormalTok{years\_of\_interest }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"2001"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2005"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2006"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2007"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2008"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2011"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2017"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2018"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2019"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"2020"}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# 2021 excluded due to no data}
\NormalTok{year\_suffixes }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{substr}\NormalTok{(years\_of\_interest, }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)  }\CommentTok{\# "01", "05", etc.}

\CommentTok{\# Order columns by year}
\NormalTok{state\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_"}\NormalTok{, year\_suffixes) }\CommentTok{\# paste0() more efficient than paste()}
\NormalTok{district\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"district\_"}\NormalTok{, year\_suffixes)}

\CommentTok{\# Interleave columns}
\NormalTok{interleaved\_renamings }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ state\_cols }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(district\_cols) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# rbind()}
  \FunctionTok{as.vector}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{interleaved\_old\_names }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(years\_of\_interest, }\StringTok{"\_STATENAME"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{rbind}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(years\_of\_interest, }\StringTok{"\_DISTNAME"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{as.vector}\NormalTok{()}

\CommentTok{\# Rename columns}
\NormalTok{column\_renamings }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{setNames}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  interleaved\_old\_names, }
\NormalTok{  interleaved\_renamings}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{district\_tracker }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp[}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{), ] }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!!!}\NormalTok{column\_renamings) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# \textasciigrave{}!!!\textasciigrave{} is the splice operator, to splice and inject arguments from a list into a function call. Note: Base R often needs inject() to accept \textasciigrave{}!!!\textasciigrave{}}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(column\_renamings)))}


\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Diagnose and correct mistakes \#\#\#\#}

\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# ...in states/UTs}

\CommentTok{\# View state/UT changes recorded in original data}
\NormalTok{district\_tracker }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{rowwise}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{unique}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c\_across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(state\_cols)))) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(state\_cols)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{invisible}\NormalTok{()}
\CommentTok{\# Two changes, both from 2019, both first reflected in the 2019 data: the union territory (UT) of Ladakh split from Jammu and Kashmir, and the UT Dadra and Nagar Haveli and Daman and Diu formed from the merger of Dadra and Nagar Haveli with Daman and Diu}
\CommentTok{\# This means four changes were not recorded in the database: renaming Pondicherry (both the district and its UT) to Puducherry in 2006, renaming Uttaranchal to Uttarakhand in 2007, renaming Orissa to Odisha in 2011, and cleaving Telangana out of Andhra Pradesh in 2014.}

\CommentTok{\# Add remaining state/UT changes}
\NormalTok{district\_tracker }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_tracker }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# For state\_xx columns with suffix \textless{} "06"}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(state\_01, district\_01, state\_05, district\_05), }
                \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(. }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Puducherry"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Pondicherry"}\NormalTok{, .))) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# For state\_xx columns with suffix \textless{} "07"}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(state\_01, state\_05, state\_06), }
                \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(. }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Uttarakhand"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Uttaranchal"}\NormalTok{, .))) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# For state\_xx columns with suffix \textless{} "11"}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(state\_01, state\_05, state\_06, state\_07, state\_08), }
                \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(. }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Odisha"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Orissa"}\NormalTok{, .))) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# For state\_xx columns with suffix \textless{} "14"}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(state\_01, state\_05, state\_06, state\_07, state\_08, state\_11), }
                \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(. }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Telangana"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Andhra Pradesh"}\NormalTok{, .)))}
\CommentTok{\# }\AlertTok{NOTE}\CommentTok{: The 07{-}08 NSS data uses Pondicherry instead of the 2006 name change of Puducherry!! They also (more understandably) use Uttaranchal instead of the 2007 name change Uttarakhand. }
\CommentTok{\#Fix: To join data from 07{-}08 NSS, must search for matches beyond the sample years.}


\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# ...in districts}

\CommentTok{\# View number of districts which changed names during a dataset\textquotesingle{}s sampling period}
\NormalTok{inperiod\_district\_changes }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_tracker }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    district\_05 }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ district\_06 }\SpecialCharTok{|}
\NormalTok{    district\_07 }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ district\_08 }\SpecialCharTok{|}
\NormalTok{    district\_17 }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ district\_18 }\SpecialCharTok{|}
\NormalTok{    district\_19 }\SpecialCharTok{!=}\NormalTok{ district\_20}
\NormalTok{  )}
\CommentTok{\# 16 districts :(}
\CommentTok{\# Fix: To join data from multi{-}year surveys (e.g., 07{-}08), we\textquotesingle{}ll need to check for matches across all sampled years at least}



\CommentTok{\# View number of districts each year with the same name despite being in different states}

\CommentTok{\# 1. Filter rows}
\CommentTok{\# For each suffix, we flag rows where the district (for that suffix) appears with more than one distinct state. Then we keep rows where at least one of the suffix comparisons is TRUE.}

\CommentTok{\# Create a list of logical vectors (one per suffix)}
\NormalTok{keep\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(year\_suffixes, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(sfx) \{}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Build the column names for this suffix}
\NormalTok{  state\_col }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_"}\NormalTok{, sfx)}
\NormalTok{  district\_col }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"district\_"}\NormalTok{, sfx)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Group the data by district for this suffix and count distinct states}
\NormalTok{  temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_tracker }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
      \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(.data[[district\_col]]),}
      \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(.data[[state\_col]])}
\NormalTok{    ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{district =}\NormalTok{ .data[[district\_col]]) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{n\_states =} \FunctionTok{n\_distinct}\NormalTok{(.data[[state\_col]], }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{.groups =} \StringTok{"drop"}
\NormalTok{    )}
  \CommentTok{\# Districts that occur with more than one unique state}
\NormalTok{  duplicate\_districts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(n\_states }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{pull}\NormalTok{(district)}
  \CommentTok{\# Return a logical vector: TRUE if the district value in the row is in duplicate\_districts}
\NormalTok{  district\_tracker[[district\_col]] }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ duplicate\_districts}
\NormalTok{\})}
\CommentTok{\# Combine the logical vectors by taking the rowwise OR (i.e., TRUE if condition holds for any suffix)}
\NormalTok{keep\_indicator }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{Reduce}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{|}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{, keep\_list)}
\CommentTok{\# Filter the original data}
\NormalTok{same\_name\_districts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ district\_tracker[keep\_indicator, ]}

\CommentTok{\# 2. Summarize by district for each suffix}
\CommentTok{\# For each suffix, group the filtered data by the district column and count:}
\CommentTok{\# a. the number of rows (n\_rows) sharing that district value, and }
\CommentTok{\# b. the number of distinct state values (n\_states) in that group.}
\CommentTok{\# Then keep only groups that have more than one unique state.}
\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(year\_suffixes, }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(sfx) \{}
\NormalTok{  state\_col }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_"}\NormalTok{, sfx)}
\NormalTok{  district\_col }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"district\_"}\NormalTok{, sfx)}
\NormalTok{  same\_name\_districts }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{district\_name =}\NormalTok{ .data[[district\_col]]) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{n\_rows =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{(),}
              \AttributeTok{n\_states =} \FunctionTok{n\_distinct}\NormalTok{(.data[[state\_col]]),}
              \AttributeTok{.groups =} \StringTok{"drop"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(n\_states }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{year\_suffix =}\NormalTok{ sfx)}
\NormalTok{\})}
\CommentTok{\# Combine summaries from all suffixes into one data frame}
\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(temp)}
\CommentTok{\# Make it easy to get summary stats}
\NormalTok{n\_same\_name\_districts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(year\_suffix) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{summarize}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{n =} \FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{())}
\CommentTok{\# Between min(n\_same\_name\_districts$n) = 3 and max(n\_same\_name\_districts$n) = 5 districts with the same name in different states in each year of interest}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section*{Chunk 7: Participation model: Cleaning and prep}\label{chunk-7-participation-model-cleaning-and-prep}

\CommentTok{\# Goal: Regress on variables which affect the probability one enrolls in or stays enrolled in school, but which do not otherwise affect district{-}level outcomes of interest (consumption, wages, etc.)}


\CommentTok{\# Collect data on those aged 5{-}19 who are in school}
\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ edu0708b5 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(AGE }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{PID =}\NormalTok{ PID,}
    \AttributeTok{district\_code =}\NormalTok{ district\_code,}

    \AttributeTok{RECD\_STATIONERY =} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
      \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(RECD\_STATIONERY }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{),}\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"No"}\NormalTok{), }
      \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"No"}\NormalTok{)), }\CommentTok{\# 151 NAs, labeled No}
    \AttributeTok{MID\_DAY\_MEAL\_ETC\_RECD =} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      MID\_DAY\_MEAL\_ETC\_RECD, }
      \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{), }
      \AttributeTok{labels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"No"}\NormalTok{)), }\CommentTok{\# No NAs}
    \AttributeTok{.keep =} \StringTok{"none"}
\NormalTok{  )}


\CommentTok{\# Merge with more data on those aged 5{-}19 who are in school}
\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ edu0708b6 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(AGE }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{PID =}\NormalTok{ PID,}
    \AttributeTok{district\_code =}\NormalTok{ district\_code,}
    \AttributeTok{enrolled =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}
    \AttributeTok{weight =}\NormalTok{ weight,}

\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}

\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{full\_join}\NormalTok{(selection\_df, temp, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{join\_by}\NormalTok{(PID, district\_code, enrolled, weight, FSU\_SL\_NO, HHID, STATE, STRATUM, SUB\_STRATUM\_NO)) }\CommentTok{\# Equivalent to excluding district\_code, enrolled, and weight; doing this, however, prevents equivalent .x and .y columns from forming (e.g., enrolled.x and enrolled.y)}


\CommentTok{\# Merge with data on all who are aged 5{-}19, including those who are not enrolled in school}
\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ edu0708b4 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(AGE }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{, AGE }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=} \DecValTok{19}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}

    \AttributeTok{SEX =} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}

\NormalTok{      RELIGION, }

    \AttributeTok{SOCIAL\_GROUP =} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      SOCIAL\_GROUP, }
      \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{,}\DecValTok{9}\NormalTok{), }

                 \StringTok{"1km \textless{}= d \textless{}2kms"}\NormalTok{,}

\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{full\_join}\NormalTok{(selection\_df, temp, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{join\_by}\NormalTok{(PID, district\_code, weight, FSU\_SL\_NO, HHID, STATE, STRATUM, SUB\_STRATUM\_NO))}




\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Father\textquotesingle{}s education proxy}
\CommentTok{\# Merge with data on father\textquotesingle{}s education}
\CommentTok{\# @azam2013a, @munshi2006a, @singh2013: Father\textquotesingle{}s education as proxy of ability. So use father\textquotesingle{}s education for father\_educ}

\CommentTok{\# Father proxy: within{-}HH male and potential parent. Defined for each HHID in this priority order:}
\CommentTok{\# Male head (RELATION\_TO\_HEAD==1 \& SEX==1)}
\CommentTok{\# Male married child of head (3 \& 1) (common for married male to live with parents)}
\CommentTok{\# Male spouse of head (2 \& 1) ***OR MAYBE 5 \& 1!!! CHANGE IN FUTURE. Misclassification error in data here.}
\CommentTok{\# Male parent/parent{-}in{-}law of head (7 \& 1)}

\CommentTok{\# Build a household{-}level "father proxy" table}
\NormalTok{father\_proxy }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ edu0708b4 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{educ\_collapsed =} \FunctionTok{fct\_collapse}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      EDUCATION\_LEVEL,}
      \AttributeTok{Illiterate =} \StringTok{"01"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Literate, no school}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}} \OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"02"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"03"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"04"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"05"}\NormalTok{),}
      \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Literate, school \textless{} primary}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}} \OtherTok{=} \StringTok{"06"}\NormalTok{,}
      \AttributeTok{Primary =} \StringTok{"07"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Upper primary}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}} \OtherTok{=} \StringTok{"08"}\NormalTok{,}
      \AttributeTok{Secondary =} \StringTok{"10"}\NormalTok{,}
      \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Higher secondary}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}} \OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"11"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"12"}\NormalTok{),}
      \StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Postsecondary+}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}} \OtherTok{=} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"13"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"14"}\NormalTok{),}
      \AttributeTok{.default =} \ConstantTok{NA\_character\_}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \CommentTok{\# priority rank (lower = better)}
    \AttributeTok{father\_rank =} \FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      RELATION\_TO\_HEAD }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ SEX }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\CommentTok{\# Male head}
\NormalTok{      RELATION\_TO\_HEAD }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{3} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ SEX }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{2}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\CommentTok{\# Male married child}
\CommentTok{\#      RELATION\_TO\_HEAD == 2 \& SEX == 1 \textasciitilde{} 3L, \# Male spouse of head; average age of this 11.3, or 11.0 after filtering for female heads. Misclassification error!}
\NormalTok{      RELATION\_TO\_HEAD }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{7} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ SEX }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{4}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{, }\CommentTok{\# Male parent/parent{-}in{-}law of head}
      \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_integer\_} \CommentTok{\# Have to specify all are ints}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(HHID) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{arrange}\NormalTok{(father\_rank, }\AttributeTok{.by\_group =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{slice}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\DataTypeTok{L}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \CommentTok{\# Best available candidate}
  \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    HHID,}
    \AttributeTok{father\_educ =} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(educ\_collapsed,}
                           \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Illiterate"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"Literate, no school"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"Literate, school \textless{} primary"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"Primary"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"Upper primary"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"Secondary"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"Higher secondary"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"Postsecondary+"}\NormalTok{)),}
    \AttributeTok{.keep =} \StringTok{"none"}
\NormalTok{  )}

\CommentTok{\# Join to selection\_df (adds the same parental\_educ to all kids in HH)}
\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(father\_proxy, }\AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"HHID"}\NormalTok{)}




\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Enrollment and NA cost removal}

\CommentTok{\# Create "enrolled" variable}
\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{district\_code\_0708 =}\NormalTok{ district\_code) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \CommentTok{\# any child not in edu0708b5/b6 gets enrolled=0}
    \AttributeTok{enrolled =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(enrolled), }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, enrolled),}
    \AttributeTok{enrolled =} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(enrolled, }\AttributeTok{levels =} \DecValTok{0}\SpecialCharTok{:}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{labels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"No"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{)),}
    \AttributeTok{district\_code\_0708 =} \FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_0708)}
\NormalTok{  )}


\CommentTok{\# Create enrollment cost. }
\CommentTok{\# Use documentation to remove some NAs (else many NAs would come from e.g., kids with RECD\_TXT\_BOOKS=="Yes" but an NA in BOOKS)}
\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \CommentTok{\# Remove some NAs: Either condition below implies free tuition, per NSS documentation}
    \AttributeTok{TUTION\_FEE =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(}
      \FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(TUTION\_FEE) }\SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ (IS\_EDU\_FREE }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"} \SpecialCharTok{|}\NormalTok{ TUTION\_FEE\_WAIVED }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{), }
      \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, TUTION\_FEE}
\NormalTok{      ),}
    \CommentTok{\# Textbooks received {-}\textgreater{} books cost 0 if missing}
    \AttributeTok{BOOKS =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(}
      \FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(BOOKS) }\SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ RECD\_TXT\_BOOKS }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{,}
      \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, BOOKS}
\NormalTok{      ),}
    \CommentTok{\# Stationery received {-}\textgreater{} stationery cost 0 if missing}
    \AttributeTok{STATIONERY =} \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(}
      \FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(STATIONERY) }\SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ RECD\_STATIONERY }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{,}
      \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, STATIONERY}
\NormalTok{      ),}
    \AttributeTok{ENROLLMENT\_COST =}\NormalTok{ TUTION\_FEE }\SpecialCharTok{+} \CommentTok{\# Same spelling as in data}
\NormalTok{                      EXAMINATION\_FEE }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{                      OTHER\_FEES\_PAYMENTS }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{                      BOOKS }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{                      STATIONERY }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{                      UNIFORM }\SpecialCharTok{+}
\NormalTok{                      TRANSPORT}
\NormalTok{  )}



\CommentTok{\# Explicitly set reference level for all factors}
\CommentTok{\# (Note that the 1st level when defining the variables is by default the reference e.g., "Hindu" was already the reference level for RELIGION):}
\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{RELIGION =} \FunctionTok{relevel}\NormalTok{(RELIGION, }\AttributeTok{ref =} \StringTok{"Hindu"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{SOCIAL\_GROUP =} \FunctionTok{relevel}\NormalTok{(SOCIAL\_GROUP, }\AttributeTok{ref =} \StringTok{"Other"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{DIST\_FROM\_NEAREST\_PRIMARY\_CLASS =} 
      \FunctionTok{relevel}\NormalTok{(DIST\_FROM\_NEAREST\_PRIMARY\_CLASS, }\AttributeTok{ref =} \StringTok{"d\textless{}1km"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{father\_educ =} \FunctionTok{relevel}\NormalTok{(father\_educ, }\AttributeTok{ref =} \StringTok{"Illiterate"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\CommentTok{\# Confirm}
\CommentTok{\# levels(selection\_df$RELIGION)}
\CommentTok{\# levels(selection\_df$SOCIAL\_GROUP)}
\CommentTok{\# levels(selection\_df$DIST\_FROM\_NEAREST\_PRIMARY\_CLASS)}
\CommentTok{\# levels(selection\_df$father\_educ)}



\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# District{-}level aggregates for imputation \#\#\#\#}

\CommentTok{\# Many relevant variables are only defined for enrolled kids. In lieu of using multiple imputation to assign them for not{-}enrolled kids, we use district{-}level aggregates of these variables as instruments for each child in the district. The exclusion restriction of the Heckman correction holds for the aggregates as it does for the original variables.}

\NormalTok{enrolled\_only\_vars }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"IS\_EDU\_FREE"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"TUTION\_FEE\_WAIVED"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"RECD\_SCHOLARSHIP\_STIPEND"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"RECD\_TXT\_BOOKS"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"RECD\_STATIONERY"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"MID\_DAY\_MEAL\_ETC\_RECD"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"ENROLLMENT\_COST"}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Ensure binary factors, ENROLLMENT\_COST are numeric}
\NormalTok{temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(enrolled\_only\_vars), }
           \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
             \CommentTok{\# for factors that are Yes/No:}
             \FunctionTok{is.factor}\NormalTok{(.x) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(.x }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{),}
             \CommentTok{\# for cost, should already be numeric:}
             \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \FunctionTok{as.numeric}\NormalTok{(.x)}
\NormalTok{             ),}
      \AttributeTok{.names=}\StringTok{"num\_\{col\}"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    )}

\CommentTok{\# Take their weighted district{-}level means}
\NormalTok{district\_agg }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(enrolled }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_0708) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{summarize}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{starts\_with}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"num\_"}\NormalTok{), }\CommentTok{\# the numeric versions}
                   \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ \{}
\NormalTok{                     val }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{weighted.mean}\NormalTok{(.x, }\AttributeTok{w=}\NormalTok{weight, }\AttributeTok{na.rm=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }
                     \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{is.nan}\NormalTok{(val)) }\ConstantTok{NA\_real\_} \ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ val }\CommentTok{\# Convert NaN (from dividing by 0, no one in district has it) to NA}
\NormalTok{                   \},}
                   \AttributeTok{.names =} \StringTok{"dmean\_\{.col\}"}\NormalTok{),}
            \AttributeTok{.groups=}\StringTok{"drop"}
\NormalTok{            )}

\CommentTok{\# For future: Use regional and state level if district level does not exist}

\CommentTok{\# Bring those means in without overwriting}
\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(district\_agg, }\AttributeTok{by=}\StringTok{"district\_code\_0708"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# May be better to give unenrolled kids the weighted average enrollment cost of enrolled kids who are a) in the same district, b) with the same values for all the probit\_controls variables, except for c) AGE, where we include kids up to two years younger and two years older? May end up with far more missing values, however.}


\CommentTok{\# Merge state names, region names}
\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  districts\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{district\_code\_0708 =} \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_0708)), }
  \AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"district\_code\_0708"}\NormalTok{)}


\CommentTok{\# Build regressor lists}
\NormalTok{probit\_controls   }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"AGE"}\NormalTok{,}
                       \StringTok{"SEX"}\NormalTok{,}
                       \StringTok{"HH\_SIZE"}\NormalTok{,}
                       \StringTok{"RELIGION"}\NormalTok{,}
                       \StringTok{"SOCIAL\_GROUP"}\NormalTok{,}
                       \StringTok{"SECTOR"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{probit\_excl\_restr\_all\_kids }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"DIST\_FROM\_NEAREST\_PRIMARY\_CLASS"}\NormalTok{,}
                       \StringTok{"father\_educ"}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{probit\_excl\_restr\_enrolled\_only }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}
  \StringTok{"dmean\_num\_IS\_EDU\_FREE"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"dmean\_num\_TUTION\_FEE\_WAIVED"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"dmean\_num\_RECD\_SCHOLARSHIP\_STIPEND"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"dmean\_num\_RECD\_TXT\_BOOKS"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"dmean\_num\_RECD\_STATIONERY"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"dmean\_num\_MID\_DAY\_MEAL\_ETC\_RECD"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"dmean\_num\_ENROLLMENT\_COST"}
\NormalTok{)}


\NormalTok{probit\_vars }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(probit\_controls, probit\_excl\_restr\_all\_kids, probit\_excl\_restr\_enrolled\_only)}

\CommentTok{\# Create formula from regressor vectors}
\NormalTok{f\_probit }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{reformulate}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  probit\_vars,}
  \AttributeTok{response =} \StringTok{"enrolled"}
\NormalTok{  )}
