\CommentTok{\#   filter(}
\CommentTok{\#     state\_0708=="Rajasthan" \&}
\CommentTok{\#       region\_0708=="Southern"}
\CommentTok{\#     ) \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   filter(if\_any(everything(),is.na)) \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   select(where(anyNA)) \%\textgreater{}\%}
\CommentTok{\#   View}
\CommentTok{\# Southern region of Rajasthan: People with one missing cost variable often have ones which aren\textquotesingle{}t missing. The person as a whole wasn\textquotesingle{}t excluded from the data.}
\CommentTok{\# Explanations: Surveyor messed up writing some costs but not others. Or surveyor meant to put a 0.  }

\CommentTok{\# Define all variables}

\CommentTok{\# Missing variables defined only for enrolled}

\NormalTok{cts\_vars }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"AGE"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"HH\_SIZE"}\NormalTok{)}




\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Correlation matrix \#\#\#\#}

\CommentTok{\# First, for all observations}
\CommentTok{\# Make new df with missingness indicator vars}
\NormalTok{temp1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(miss\_vars\_all), }
           \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(.)),}
           \AttributeTok{.names =} \StringTok{"miss\_\{.col\}"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{.keep =} \StringTok{"none"}
\NormalTok{  )}
\CommentTok{\# Expand factors to set of dummy variables}
\NormalTok{temp2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{model.matrix}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{.}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(group\_vars))) }\CommentTok{\# {-}1 removes intercept column}
\CommentTok{\# Compute correlation matrix}
\NormalTok{sel\_corr\_mat\_all }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{cor}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{cbind}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    temp1, }
\NormalTok{    selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(cts\_vars)), }
\NormalTok{    temp2}
\NormalTok{    ),}
  \AttributeTok{use =} \StringTok{"pairwise.complete.obs"} \CommentTok{\# Corr found for complete pairs. NA entries allowed. Pearson method.}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Second, only for enrolled observations}
\CommentTok{\# Make new df with missingness indicator vars}
\NormalTok{temp1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(enrolled}\SpecialCharTok{==}\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{across}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(miss\_vars\_enrolled), }
           \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(.)),}
           \AttributeTok{.names =} \StringTok{"miss\_\{.col\}"}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{.keep =} \StringTok{"none"}
\NormalTok{  )}
\CommentTok{\# Expand factors to set of dummy variables}
\NormalTok{temp2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{model.matrix}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{.}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }
                      \AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(enrolled}\SpecialCharTok{==}\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(group\_vars)),}
                      \AttributeTok{na.action=}\NormalTok{na.pass}
\NormalTok{                      )}
\CommentTok{\# Compute correlation matrix}
\NormalTok{sel\_corr\_mat\_enrolled }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{cor}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{cbind}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    temp1, }
\NormalTok{    selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(enrolled}\SpecialCharTok{==}\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(cts\_vars)), }
\NormalTok{    temp2}
\NormalTok{    ),}
  \AttributeTok{use =} \StringTok{"pairwise.complete.obs"} \CommentTok{\# Corr found for complete pairs. Allows for NA entries. Pearson method.}
\NormalTok{)}

\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Logistic per missing variable \#\#\#\#}

\NormalTok{check\_missing\_logit\_parallel }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(df, miss\_vars, covars, }\AttributeTok{method\_p =} \StringTok{"BH"}\NormalTok{) \{}

    \CommentTok{\# Return tidy df of coefficients and attach missing var\textquotesingle{}s name}

      \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}

  \CommentTok{\# Parallelization}
  \CommentTok{\# Cluster with parLapply() if on Windows}
\NormalTok{  out\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (.Platform}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{OS.type }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"windows"}\NormalTok{) \{}

\NormalTok{  parallel}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{clusterEvalQ}\NormalTok{(cl, \{}
    \FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(broom)}
    \FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(dplyr)}
\NormalTok{  \})}
\NormalTok{  parallel}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{clusterExport}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    cl,}
    \AttributeTok{varlist =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"rhs"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"fit\_one"}\NormalTok{),}

\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{ }\CommentTok{\# Fork with mclapply()}
\NormalTok{    parallel}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{mclapply}\NormalTok{(miss\_vars, fit\_one, }\AttributeTok{mc.cores =} \FunctionTok{max}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, parallel}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{detectCores}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{{-}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{))}

\NormalTok{  out }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ out }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(missing\_var) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}

      \AttributeTok{p\_adj =}\NormalTok{ \{ }\CommentTok{\# Adjust within each missingness model}
\NormalTok{        adj }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{NA\_real\_}\NormalTok{, dplyr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{n}\NormalTok{())}

\NormalTok{        adj}
\NormalTok{      \}}
\NormalTok{      ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{() }
\NormalTok{  out}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Run on missing variables defined for all children}

\CommentTok{\# "BY" lets independence or positive dependence assumptions weaken to arbitrary dependence, but has weaker power (i.e., more p{-}vals above 0.05).}

\section*{Chunk 9: Participation model: Estimation and IMR}\label{chunk-9-participation-model-estimation-and-imr}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 9: Participation model: Estimation and IMR}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Handling lonely PSUs ("variance formula  gives 0/0 if stratum contains only one sampling unit", \textasciigrave{}?svyCprod\textasciigrave{})}
\CommentTok{\# Ex: The "Jhelam Valley" stratum has only one PSU in the data.}

\CommentTok{\# Options: ""fail" to give an error, "remove" or "certainty" to give a variance contribution of 0 for the stratum, "adjust" to center the stratum at the grand mean rather than the stratum mean, and "average" to assign strata with one PSU the average variance contribution from strata with more than one PSU."}
\CommentTok{\# ""adjust" is conservative, and it would often be better to combine strata in some intelligent way."}
\CommentTok{\# "properties of "average" have not been investigated thoroughly, but it may be useful when the lonely PSUs are due to a few strata having PSUs missing completely at random."}
\CommentTok{\# ""remove" and "certainty" options give the same result" }
\CommentTok{\# "but "certainty" is intended for situations where there is only one PSU in the population stratum, which is sampled with certainty (also called ‘self{-}representing’ PSUs or strata). With "certainty" no warning is generated for strata with only one PSU. Ordinarily, svydesign will detect certainty PSUs, making this option unnecessary."}

\CommentTok{\# Will thus use "average" for handling single{-}PSU strata (e.g., "Jhelam Valley") when estimating variance}
\FunctionTok{options}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{survey.lonely.psu =} \StringTok{"average"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Create weighted survey design model}
\NormalTok{selection\_design }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{svydesign}\NormalTok{(}
  
  \AttributeTok{ids =} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{FSU\_SL\_NO }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ HHID, }
  \CommentTok{\# \textasciigrave{}?svydesign\textasciigrave{}: "For multistage sampling the id argument should specify a formula with the cluster identifiers at each stage."}
  \CommentTok{\# Sampling occurred in two stages: the first{-}stage units (FSU) were rural villages/urban blocks (FSU\_SL\_NO), and the ultimate stage units (USUs) were households (HHID)}
  
  \AttributeTok{strata =} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\FunctionTok{interaction}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(STATE),}
    \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(STRATUM),}
    \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(SUB\_STRATUM\_NO),}
    \AttributeTok{drop =} \ConstantTok{TRUE} \CommentTok{\# Nothing dropped yet}
\NormalTok{    ), }
  \CommentTok{\# Sampling stratified into state, stratum (district), and substratum (rural/urban, with multiple urban substrata if population dense enough)}

  \AttributeTok{weights =} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{weight,}
  \AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ selection\_df,}
  
  \AttributeTok{nest =} \ConstantTok{TRUE} \CommentTok{\# Clusters (PSUs) are nested within strata (states*strata*substrata)}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Estimate weighted model}
\NormalTok{model\_probit\_selection }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{svyglm}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  f\_probit,}
  \AttributeTok{design =}\NormalTok{ selection\_design,}
  \AttributeTok{family =} \FunctionTok{binomial}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{link =} \StringTok{"probit"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# Rows with an NA for a probit{-}relevant variable dropped!}



\CommentTok{\# Derive IMR}
\CommentTok{\# For now, calculate IMR for all rows. Don\textquotesingle{}t drop rows with NAs in unrelated columns:}

\CommentTok{\# Rows with no NA under probit{-}relevant variable}
\NormalTok{needed\_vars }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{all.vars}\NormalTok{(f\_probit) }\CommentTok{\# = c(probit\_vars, "enrolled") }

\CommentTok{\# Take only complete cases of variables in f\_probit}
\NormalTok{comp\_cases }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{complete.cases}\NormalTok{(selection\_df[, needed\_vars, }\AttributeTok{drop =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{])}

\CommentTok{\# Predict only on complete rows; NA for rest}
\NormalTok{lp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{NA\_real\_}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(selection\_df)) }\CommentTok{\# full{-}length placeholders}
\NormalTok{lp[comp\_cases] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{predict}\NormalTok{(model\_probit\_selection,}
                         \AttributeTok{newdata =}\NormalTok{ selection\_df[comp\_cases, , }\AttributeTok{drop=}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{],}
                         \AttributeTok{type =} \StringTok{"link"}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# to return linear predictors}

\CommentTok{\# Build IMR}
\NormalTok{phi\_lp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{dnorm}\NormalTok{(lp)}
\NormalTok{Phi\_lp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{pnorm}\NormalTok{(lp)}

\CommentTok{\# Remaining NAs could be from dividing by 0. }
\CommentTok{\# Ensure against this by keeping Phi\_lp \textbackslash{}in (0,1) strictly}
\NormalTok{Phi\_lp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{pmin}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{pmax}\NormalTok{(Phi\_lp, .Machine}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{double.eps), }\DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ .Machine}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{double.eps)}
\CommentTok{\# .Machine$double.eps = 2.220446e{-}16 on my device}

\NormalTok{selection\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{IMR =} \FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      enrolled }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ phi\_lp }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ Phi\_lp,}
\NormalTok{      enrolled }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"No"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{phi\_lp }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ (}\DecValTok{1} \SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ Phi\_lp),}
      \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_real\_} \CommentTok{\# NA if missing predictor}
\NormalTok{      )}
\NormalTok{  )}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section*{Chunk 10: Participation model: Derive AME}\label{chunk-10-participation-model-derive-ame}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 10: Participation model: Derive AME}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Use automatic differentiation (AD) for SE delta method gradients}
\FunctionTok{autodiff}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{autodiff =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{install =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# install=TRUE if self{-}managing Python install}
\FunctionTok{options}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{marginaleffects\_parallel =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# Make sure it\textquotesingle{}s off}
\NormalTok{sel\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ selection\_df[comp\_cases, , drop }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{]}

\NormalTok{num\_samp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{200}
\FunctionTok{set.seed}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{999}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{final\_draft }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ConstantTok{TRUE} \CommentTok{\# Set TRUE when rendering final draft}
\NormalTok{newdata\_ame }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (final\_draft) sel\_data }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ sel\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{slice\_sample}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{n =}\NormalTok{ num\_samp)}

\CommentTok{\# start.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\NormalTok{mfx\_all }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{avg\_slopes}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  model\_probit\_selection,}
  \AttributeTok{newdata =}\NormalTok{ newdata\_ame,}
  \AttributeTok{wts =} \StringTok{"weight"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{vcov =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\CommentTok{\# Set FALSE to make this even faster}
  \AttributeTok{type =} \StringTok{"response"}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# end.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# tdiff \textless{}{-} end.time {-} start.time}
\CommentTok{\# \# With newdata = sel\_data (no subsampling, as if num\_samp = 279180): 6.178544{-}11.17861 mins when ran for the first time, 4.853338 mins later.}
\CommentTok{\# \# With num\_samp = 20000: 36.13833 secs}
\CommentTok{\# \# With num\_samp = 2000: 4.005744 secs}



\CommentTok{\# The rest of this chunk is saved for quick replications of robustness checks on my final method}

\CommentTok{\# Raw AME derivation is very slow: }
\CommentTok{\# 9 numeric variables * 279180 observations * 2 calls of predict() per observation per variable (avg\_slopes() uses centered finite difference, see https://marginaleffects.com/bonus/uncertainty.html\#numerical{-}derivatives{-}sensitivity{-}to{-}step{-}size) = 5025240 predict() calls. }

\CommentTok{\# Method 1: Straight Sampling and Subsampling }
\CommentTok{\# Note: "slopes() functions will automatically revert to comparisons() for binary or categorical variables" (https://marginaleffects.com/man/r/slopes.html)}

\CommentTok{\# num\_samp \textless{}{-} 2000}
\CommentTok{\# set.seed(999)}
\CommentTok{\# newdata\_ame \textless{}{-} sel\_data \%\textgreater{}\% slice\_sample(n = num\_samp)}
\CommentTok{\# \# newdata\_ame \textless{}{-} sel\_data}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# start.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# mfx\_all \textless{}{-} avg\_slopes(}
\CommentTok{\#   model\_probit\_selection,}
\CommentTok{\#   newdata = newdata\_ame,}
\CommentTok{\#   wts = "weight",}
\CommentTok{\#   vcov = TRUE \# Set as FALSE to make this even faster}
\CommentTok{\# )}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# end.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# end.time {-} start.time}

\CommentTok{\# With newdata = sel\_data (no subsampling, as if num\_samp = 279180): \textasciitilde{}40 minutes!}
\CommentTok{\# With num\_samp = 20000: 36.7708 secs}
\CommentTok{\# With num\_samp = 2000: 4.429373 secs}

\CommentTok{\# Method 2: Subsampling with forward differences}
\CommentTok{\# Note: Calls predict() once per perturbation instead of twice (a la central differences, "fdcenter")}
\CommentTok{\# Run the above, but add numderiv = "fdforward" into avg\_slopes()}
\CommentTok{\# With num\_samp = 20000: 37.41933 secs}
\CommentTok{\# With num\_samp = 2000: 4.047509 secs}
\CommentTok{\# Cheaper numeric differentiation didn\textquotesingle{}t help at all! Reflective of how many discrete variables I have.}
\CommentTok{\# Centered differences are generally more accurate than forward differences for continuous vars}

\CommentTok{\# Method 3: Split slopes and comparisons, just to be sure}
\CommentTok{\# Ran avg\_slopes on numeric\_vars, avg\_comparisons on factor\_vars}
\CommentTok{\# With num\_samp = 20000: 38.94813 secs}
\CommentTok{\# With num\_samp = 2000: 5.039992 secs}
\CommentTok{\# No. Just use avg\_slopes()}


\CommentTok{\# Method 4: Parallelization}

\CommentTok{\# library(future.apply) \# For parallelization}
\CommentTok{\# \# }
\CommentTok{\# \# Resolve futures in parallel in *forked* R processes. NOT SUPPORTED ON WINDOWS!}
\CommentTok{\# plan(multicore, workers = 4) \# Using "multisession" led to the same result.}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# options(marginaleffects\_parallel = TRUE) \# parallelize delta method computation of standard errors}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# num\_samp = 2000}
\CommentTok{\# set.seed(999)}
\CommentTok{\# newdata\_ame \textless{}{-} sel\_data \%\textgreater{}\% slice\_sample(n = num\_samp)}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# start.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# mfx\_all \textless{}{-} avg\_slopes(}
\CommentTok{\#   model\_probit\_selection,}
\CommentTok{\#   newdata = newdata\_ame,}
\CommentTok{\#   wts = "weight",}
\CommentTok{\#   vcov = TRUE \# Set as FALSE to make this even faster}
\CommentTok{\# )}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# end.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# end.time {-} start.time}

\CommentTok{\# Failed! "The total size of the 18 globals exported for future expression (‘FUN()’) is 7.90 GiB." Three largest globals: "‘FUN’ (3.54 GiB of class ‘function’), ‘func’ (3.54 GiB of class ‘function’) and ‘mfx’ (544.70 MiB of class ‘S4’)."}

\CommentTok{\# As documentation states: "There is always considerable overhead when using parallel computation, mainly involved in passing the whole dataset to the different processes." (https://cloud.r{-}project.org/web/packages/marginaleffects/refman/marginaleffects.html)}


\CommentTok{\# To parallelize for the whole dataset after running \textasciigrave{}environment(model\_probit\_selection) \textless{}{-} NULL; model\_probit\_selection$survey.design \textless{}{-} NULL; model\_probit\_selection$data \textless{}{-} NULL\textasciigrave{}: }
\CommentTok{\# 53.96 GiB. "The three largest globals are ‘FUN’ (24.00 GiB of class ‘function’), ‘func’ (24.00 GiB of class ‘function’) and ‘hi’ (1.82 GiB of class ‘list’)"}

\CommentTok{\# My laptop has 24 GB of RAM! So no parallelization.}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\NormalTok{  )) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}

\CommentTok{\# Preliminary test of IV strength:}
\CommentTok{\# Dotplot of EMIE values by district\_code}
\NormalTok{plt\_EMI\_across\_stats\_and\_districts }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{ggplot}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  df0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{district\_prefix =} \FunctionTok{substr}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(district\_code\_0708), }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}

  \FunctionTok{aes}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x =}\NormalTok{ district\_code\_0708, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ EMIE, }\AttributeTok{color =}\NormalTok{ district\_prefix)}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{+}

  \FunctionTok{labs}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{title =} \StringTok{"Percentage of Students in EMI by District, 2007{-}08"}\NormalTok{,}
       \AttributeTok{x =} \StringTok{"District (sorted by state and within{-}state region)"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{y =} \StringTok{"Percentage in EMI"}\NormalTok{,}
       \AttributeTok{color =} \StringTok{"State Code"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{+}
  \FunctionTok{theme\_minimal}\NormalTok{()}
\CommentTok{\# EMIE has three peaks: in Jammu and Kashmir; in Sikkim, Arunachal Pradesh, Nagaland, Manipur, Mizoran, Tripura, maybe Meghalaya; and in Andhra Pradesh, Karnataka, Goa, Lakshadweep, Kerala, Tamil Nadu, Pondicheri, and Andaman \& Nicobar! The regions which historically were the furthest from Hindi!}
\CommentTok{\# Many districts in the second group seem to have EMIE around 1, and the range of EMIE outside peaks is between 0.4 and 0.1. Justification for looking at smaller units of analysis?}



\CommentTok{\# Process the dataframe and compute the weighted average ling\_distance for each (state, district) group.}
\NormalTok{mother\_tongues\_01 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ census01 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# Group by state and district to ensure that same district names in different states are treated separately}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(state, district) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# For each group, keep only the top three rows by spkr\_tot}
  \FunctionTok{slice\_max}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{order\_by =}\NormalTok{ spkr\_tot, }\AttributeTok{n =} \DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# Ungroup before applying new transformations}
  \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# Create the ling\_distance column based on the mother\_tongue values and @shastry2012a\textquotesingle{}s 0{-}5 measure of degrees of linguistic distance}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{ling\_degrees =} \FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      mother\_tongue }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Hindi"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Urdu"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{      mother\_tongue }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Gujarati"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Punjabi"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Rajasthani"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{      mother\_tongue }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Konkani"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Marathi"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{      mother\_tongue }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Assamese"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Bengali"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Bihari"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Oriya"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, }\CommentTok{\# Oriya was renamed as Odia in 2011}
\NormalTok{      mother\_tongue }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Kashmiri"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Sindhi"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Sinhalese"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{,}
      \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \DecValTok{5} \CommentTok{\# Why TRUE?}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# Group again by state and district to compute group summaries}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(state, district) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \CommentTok{\# Calculate the weighted average ling\_distance for each group. For each langauge $\textbackslash{}ell$ which is among the top three most spoken in district $d$: $$\textbackslash{}frac\{\textbackslash{}sum\_\{\textbackslash{}ell\}(\textbackslash{}text\{linguistic distance of \}\textbackslash{}ell \textbackslash{}times \textbackslash{}text\{num. speakers of \}\textbackslash{}ell\textbackslash{}text\{ in \}d)\}\{\textbackslash{}sum\_\{\textbackslash{}ell\}(\textbackslash{}text\{num. speakers of \}\textbackslash{}ell)\}$$}
  \FunctionTok{summarize}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{wavg\_ling\_degrees =} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(ling\_degrees }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ spkr\_tot, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{/} \FunctionTok{sum}\NormalTok{(spkr\_tot, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{.groups =} \StringTok{"drop"} \CommentTok{\# Makes ungroup() redundant?}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{rename}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{state\_01 =}\NormalTok{ state, }\AttributeTok{district\_01 =}\NormalTok{ district)}

\CommentTok{\# census01 \%\textgreater{}\% mutate(StateDistrict = paste0(state\_code, district\_code)) \%\textgreater{}\% distinct(StateDistrict) \%\textgreater{}\% nrow() {-} mother\_tongues\_01 \%\textgreater{}\% mutate(StateDistrict = paste0(state\_01, district\_01)) \%\textgreater{}\% distinct(StateDistrict) \%\textgreater{}\% nrow()}
\CommentTok{\# Number of districts did not change in this operation}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Number of rows from fuzzy full joining district\_tracker (734 rows) and mother\_tongues\_01 (593 rows) with different metrics:}

\CommentTok{\# Testing different methods of fuzzy joining}

\CommentTok{\# \# With ("lcs","osa"), (3, 3):}
\CommentTok{\# colSums(is.na(joined\_df))}
\CommentTok{\# \# 75 NAs in 01 columns, 124 in 07{-}08, 105 in 17{-}18}
\CommentTok{\# sum(apply(joined\_df, 1, anyNA))}
\CommentTok{\# \# 189/734 rows have an NA}
\CommentTok{\# }

\CommentTok{\# \# 180/734}
\CommentTok{\# }

\CommentTok{\# colSums(is.na(joined\_df))}

\CommentTok{\# \# 0}
\CommentTok{\# stringdist("East Godavari", "Godavari East", method = "jaccard")}
\CommentTok{\# \# 0}


\NormalTok{evaluate\_distances }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(pairs,}
\NormalTok{                               methods, thresholds,}
                               \AttributeTok{col1 =} \StringTok{"str1"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{col2 =} \StringTok{"str2"}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(methods) }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(thresholds)) \{}
    \FunctionTok{stop}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{methods}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{ and }\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{thresholds}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}"}\StringTok{ must have the same length."}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  \CommentTok{\# Ensure chr type}
\NormalTok{  pairs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ pairs }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
      \SpecialCharTok{!!}\AttributeTok{col1 :=} \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(.data[[col1]]),}
      \SpecialCharTok{!!}\AttributeTok{col2 :=} \FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(.data[[col2]])}
\NormalTok{    )}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Compute distances for each method}
\NormalTok{  out }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(}
    \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{seq\_along}\NormalTok{(methods), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(i) \{}
\NormalTok{      m  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ methods[i]}
\NormalTok{      th }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ thresholds[i]}
      
\NormalTok{      pairs }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
        \FunctionTok{transmute}\NormalTok{(}
          \AttributeTok{str1 =}\NormalTok{ .data[[col1]],}
          \AttributeTok{str2 =}\NormalTok{ .data[[col2]],}
          \AttributeTok{method =}\NormalTok{ m,}
          \AttributeTok{distance =} \FunctionTok{stringdist}\NormalTok{(str1, str2, }\AttributeTok{method =}\NormalTok{ m),}
          \AttributeTok{threshold =}\NormalTok{ th,}
          \AttributeTok{match =}\NormalTok{ distance }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=}\NormalTok{ th}
\NormalTok{        )}
\NormalTok{    \})}
\NormalTok{  )}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Keep a consistent ordering}
\NormalTok{  out }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{arrange}\NormalTok{(str1, str2, method)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Some sample pairs}
\NormalTok{pairs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{tribble}\NormalTok{(}
  \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{str1, }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{str2,}
  \StringTok{"Baleshwar"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Balasore"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Jammu \& Kashmir"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Jammu and Kashmir"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"East Godavari"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Godavari East"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Sikim"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Sikkim"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Mumbai"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Mumbai"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"24{-}Parganas ( North )"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"North Twenty Four Parganas"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"North Twenty Four Pargan*"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"North Twenty Four Parganas"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Sahibzada Ajit Singh Nag*"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Sahibzada Ajit Singh Nagar"}\NormalTok{,}
  \StringTok{"Sri Potti Sriramulu Nell*"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Sri Potti Sriramulu Nellore"}
\NormalTok{)}


\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Helper vectors \#\#\#\#}
\NormalTok{methods }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"soundex"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"qgram"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"jw"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"dl"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"osa"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{thresholds }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{, }\FloatTok{0.15}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{\# soundex=0 {-}{-}\textgreater{} Phonetic variants in anglicization allowed (if coarsely measured)}
\CommentTok{\# qgram = 0 {-}{-}\textgreater{} Some rearrangements of characters allowed}
\CommentTok{\# jw\textless{}=0.15 {-}{-}\textgreater{} Respellings + vowel swaps with 0.85 similarity allowed}
\CommentTok{\# dl\textless{}=2 {-}{-}\textgreater{} \textless{}=2 insertions + deletions + substitutions + transpositions allowed}
\CommentTok{\# osa\textless{}=1 {-}{-}\textgreater{} 1 typo allowed}
\CommentTok{\# Template for testing these vs. other methods/thresholds can be found at start of chunk}


\CommentTok{\# Evaluate distances and test joining methods}
\CommentTok{\# colSums(is.na(joined\_df))}
\CommentTok{\# \# 53 in 01, 112 in 07{-}08, 89 in 17{-}18}
\CommentTok{\# sum(apply(joined\_df, 1, anyNA))}
\CommentTok{\# \# 166/734}
\CommentTok{\# evaluate\_distances(pairs, methods, thresholds)}
\end{Highlighting}

\section*{Chunk 17: Match districts: Define joining functions}\label{chunk-17-match-districts-define-joining-functions}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 17: Match districts: Define joining functions}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# A. Loop over the methods*thresholds}
\CommentTok{\# B. For each methods*thresholds pair, fuzzy full join all still‑unmatched rows}
\CommentTok{\# C. Return joined, unmatched\_df1, unmatched\_df2}
\NormalTok{fuzzy\_join\_sequence }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(df1, df2,}
\NormalTok{                                dist1, state1,}
\NormalTok{                                dist2, state2,}
\NormalTok{                                methods, thresholds, }\AttributeTok{mode =} \StringTok{"full"}\NormalTok{) \{}
  \CommentTok{\# Attach row IDs to track unmatched}
\NormalTok{  df1\_id }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df1 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{.id1 =} \FunctionTok{row\_number}\NormalTok{())}
\NormalTok{  df2\_id }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df2 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{.id2 =} \FunctionTok{row\_number}\NormalTok{())}
  
\NormalTok{  df1\_curr }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df1\_id}
\NormalTok{  df2\_curr }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df2\_id}
\NormalTok{  matched\_all }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{tibble}\NormalTok{()}
  
  \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{(i }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{seq\_along}\NormalTok{(methods)) \{}
\NormalTok{    full\_j }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{stringdist\_join}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{      df1\_curr, df2\_curr,}
      \AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{setNames}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(dist2, state2), }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(dist1, state1)),}
      \AttributeTok{mode =}\NormalTok{ mode,}
      \AttributeTok{method =}\NormalTok{ methods[i],}
      \AttributeTok{max\_dist =}\NormalTok{ thresholds[i],}
      \AttributeTok{distance\_col =} \StringTok{"dist"}
\NormalTok{    )}
    
    \CommentTok{\# Keep only pairs (i.e., those with both sides present) and rank them}
\NormalTok{    matched\_i }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ full\_j }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(.id1) }\SpecialCharTok{\&} \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(.id2)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(.id1) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \FunctionTok{slice\_min}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{order\_by =}\NormalTok{ dist, }\AttributeTok{n =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{with\_ties =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(.id2) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \FunctionTok{slice\_min}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{order\_by =}\NormalTok{ dist, }\AttributeTok{n =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{with\_ties =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
      \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{    matched\_all }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(matched\_all, matched\_i)}
    
    \CommentTok{\# Remove them from the to‑do sets}
\NormalTok{    df1\_curr }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df1\_curr }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{(.id1 }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ matched\_i}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{.id1))}
\NormalTok{    df2\_curr }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df2\_curr }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{(.id2 }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ matched\_i}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{.id2))}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
  \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{joined =}\NormalTok{ matched\_all,}
    \AttributeTok{unmatched\_df1 =}\NormalTok{ df1\_curr }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{.id1),}
    \AttributeTok{unmatched\_df2 =}\NormalTok{ df2\_curr }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{.id2)}
\NormalTok{  )}
\NormalTok{\}}
\CommentTok{\# Default is full join so that this can be used for both matching and diagnostics}


\CommentTok{\# For each df name in input vector:}
\CommentTok{\# A. Extract its "01"/"05"/... suffix}
\CommentTok{\# B. Find the suffix’s district\_/state\_ columns in joined\_df. }
\CommentTok{\# C. Run the fuzzy join sequence on each column. (Recall justification of fuzzy joining states in Chunk 6: Match districts: Construct district tracking dfs.)}
\CommentTok{\# D. Repeat with the predecessor suffix.}
\NormalTok{merge\_dfs\_into\_tracker }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  dfs,}
\NormalTok{  tracker,}
\NormalTok{  years\_of\_interest,}
\NormalTok{  methods, thresholds,}
  \AttributeTok{flag =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}
\NormalTok{) \{}
  \CommentTok{\# 1. Initialize both joined\_df and (if flag=TRUE) flagged\_df}
\NormalTok{  joined\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ tracker}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (flag) \{}
\NormalTok{    flagged\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ tracker}
    \CommentTok{\# Prepare placeholder vector for each df{-}name}
\NormalTok{    matched\_lists }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(dfs), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(x) }\FunctionTok{rep}\NormalTok{(}\ConstantTok{NA\_character\_}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(tracker)))}
    \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(matched\_lists) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(dfs)}
\NormalTok{  \}}

\NormalTok{  year\_suffixes }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{substr}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(years\_of\_interest), }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  unmatched\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{vector}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"list"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(dfs))}
  \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(unmatched\_list) }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(dfs)}

  \CommentTok{\# 2. Loop over each auxiliary data{-}frame name}
  \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (d\_name }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(dfs)) \{}
\NormalTok{    df\_d }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ dfs[[d\_name]]}
\NormalTok{    suffix }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ stringr}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{str\_extract}\NormalTok{(d\_name, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{d\{2\}$"}\NormalTok{)}
    \FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(suffix))}

    \CommentTok{\# Find exactly one district\_XX / state\_XX in df\_d}
\NormalTok{    dist\_d  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}district\_"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(df\_d), }\AttributeTok{value=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
                \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"code"}\NormalTok{, ., }\AttributeTok{invert=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{value=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    state\_d }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}state\_"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(df\_d), }\AttributeTok{value=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
                \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"code"}\NormalTok{, ., }\AttributeTok{invert=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{value=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
    \FunctionTok{stopifnot}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(dist\_d)}\SpecialCharTok{==}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(state\_d)}\SpecialCharTok{==}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{    df\_unmatched }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df\_d}
    \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (flag) mv }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ matched\_lists[[d\_name]]}

    \CommentTok{\# suffix\_chain sorted by absolute distance from said suffix}
\NormalTok{    year\_nums  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(year\_suffixes)}
\NormalTok{    suffix\_num }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(suffix)}
\NormalTok{    order\_idx  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{order}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{abs}\NormalTok{(year\_nums }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ suffix\_num))}
\NormalTok{    suffix\_chain }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ year\_suffixes[order\_idx]}

    \CommentTok{\# Work through suffixes, closest to furthest}
    \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (suf }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ suffix\_chain) \{}
\NormalTok{      dist\_cols\_j  }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}district\_"}\NormalTok{, suf, }\StringTok{"(?:$|\_)"}\NormalTok{),}
                           \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(joined\_df), }\AttributeTok{value=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{      state\_cols\_j }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}state\_"}\NormalTok{, suf, }\StringTok{"(?:$|\_)"}\NormalTok{),}
                           \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(joined\_df), }\AttributeTok{value=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

      \ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{ (dist\_col\_j }\ControlFlowTok{in}\NormalTok{ dist\_cols\_j) \{}
\NormalTok{        ending }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sub}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}district\_"}\NormalTok{, suf), }\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{, dist\_col\_j)}
\NormalTok{        state\_col\_j }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_"}\NormalTok{, suf, ending)}
        \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\SpecialCharTok{!}\NormalTok{state\_col\_j }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%}\NormalTok{ state\_cols\_j) }\ControlFlowTok{next}

        \CommentTok{\# 2a. Multi{-}threshold fuzzy join}
\NormalTok{        res }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{fuzzy\_join\_sequence}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{          df\_unmatched, joined\_df,}
          \AttributeTok{dist1 =}\NormalTok{ dist\_d, }
          \AttributeTok{state1 =}\NormalTok{ state\_d,}
          \AttributeTok{dist2 =}\NormalTok{ dist\_col\_j,}
          \AttributeTok{state2 =}\NormalTok{ state\_col\_j,}
          \AttributeTok{methods =}\NormalTok{ methods,}
          \AttributeTok{thresholds =}\NormalTok{ thresholds,}
          \AttributeTok{mode =} \StringTok{"full"}
\NormalTok{        )}

        \CommentTok{\# 2b. Pull other cols into joined\_df}
\NormalTok{        other\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{setdiff}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(df\_d), }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(dist\_d, state\_d))}
        \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{joined)}\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\DecValTok{0} \SpecialCharTok{\&\&} \FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(other\_cols)}\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
\NormalTok{          extra }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{joined }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(.id2, }\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{intersect}\NormalTok{(other\_cols, }\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{joined)))) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{arrange}\NormalTok{(dist, .id2) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(.id2) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{slice\_min}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{order\_by =}\NormalTok{ dist, }\AttributeTok{n =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{with\_ties =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}

          \CommentTok{\# Merge into joined\_df}
\NormalTok{          joined\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ joined\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{.row =} \FunctionTok{row\_number}\NormalTok{()) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(extra, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{".row"}\OtherTok{=}\StringTok{".id2"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{.row)}

          \CommentTok{\# If flag, merge into flagged\_df}
          \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (flag) \{}
\NormalTok{            flagged\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ flagged\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
              \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{.row =} \FunctionTok{row\_number}\NormalTok{()) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
              \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(extra, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{".row"}\OtherTok{=}\StringTok{".id2"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
              \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{.row)}
\NormalTok{          \}}
\NormalTok{        \}}

        \CommentTok{\# 2c. If flag=TRUE, record which district got matched this iteration}
        \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (flag }\SpecialCharTok{\&\&} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{joined)}\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
\NormalTok{          col\_match }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{grep}\NormalTok{(}
            \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}"}\NormalTok{, dist\_d, }\StringTok{"(?:$|}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}\textbackslash{}}\StringTok{.x$)"}\NormalTok{),}
            \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{joined), }\AttributeTok{value=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}
\NormalTok{          )[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{          info }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{joined[, }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{".id2"}\NormalTok{, col\_match), drop}\OtherTok{=}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{]}
          \FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(info)[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \StringTok{"match\_dist"}
\NormalTok{          info }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ info }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(.id2) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{slice\_head}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{n =} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
            \FunctionTok{ungroup}\NormalTok{()}

\NormalTok{          idx }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ info}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{.id2}
\NormalTok{          new\_vals }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ info}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{match\_dist}
\NormalTok{          blank }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{is.na}\NormalTok{(mv[idx])}
\NormalTok{          mv[idx[blank]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ new\_vals[blank]}
\NormalTok{        \}}

        \CommentTok{\# 2d. Update the df of unmatched}
\NormalTok{        df\_unmatched }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ res}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{unmatched\_df1}
        \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_unmatched)}\SpecialCharTok{==}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) }\ControlFlowTok{break}
\NormalTok{      \}}
      \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_unmatched)}\SpecialCharTok{==}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) }\ControlFlowTok{break}
\NormalTok{    \}}

    \CommentTok{\# 2e. Once done, append flag{-}column to flagged\_df}
    \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (flag) \{}
\NormalTok{      flagged\_df[[d\_name]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ mv}
\NormalTok{    \}}
\NormalTok{    unmatched\_list[[d\_name]] }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ df\_unmatched}
    \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(df\_unmatched)}\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}}\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{) \{}
      \FunctionTok{warning}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{sprintf}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Some rows in \%s were never matched"}\NormalTok{, d\_name))}
\NormalTok{    \}}
\NormalTok{  \}}

  \CommentTok{\# 3. Finalize flagged\_df if flag=TRUE}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (flag) \{}
\NormalTok{    max\_suf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ year\_suffixes[}\FunctionTok{which.max}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.integer}\NormalTok{(year\_suffixes))]}
\NormalTok{    keep\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(flagged\_df)[}
\NormalTok{      (}\FunctionTok{grepl}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\^{}district\_"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(flagged\_df)) }\SpecialCharTok{\&} \SpecialCharTok{!}\FunctionTok{grepl}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"code"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(flagged\_df))) }\SpecialCharTok{|}
      \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(flagged\_df) }\SpecialCharTok{\%in\%} \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(dfs) }\SpecialCharTok{|}
      \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(flagged\_df) }\SpecialCharTok{==} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_"}\NormalTok{, max\_suf)}
\NormalTok{    ]}
\NormalTok{    flagged\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ flagged\_df[, keep\_cols, drop}\OtherTok{=}\ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{  \}}

  \CommentTok{\# 4. Return!!!}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (flag) \{}
    \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{joined\_df =}\NormalTok{ joined\_df,}
      \AttributeTok{unmatched =}\NormalTok{ unmatched\_list,}
      \AttributeTok{flagged\_df =}\NormalTok{ flagged\_df}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
    \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{joined\_df =}\NormalTok{ joined\_df,}
      \AttributeTok{unmatched =}\NormalTok{ unmatched\_list}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\section*{Chunk 20: Match districts: Diagnose errors}\label{chunk-20-match-districts-diagnose-errors}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 20: Match districts: Diagnose errors}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Errors are fixed in Chunk 18: Match districts: Manually fix errors}

\CommentTok{\# Change dfs for diagnostic purposes, if desired}
\NormalTok{dfs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{list}\NormalTok{(mother\_tongues\_01, df0708, df1718, districts\_20)}

\CommentTok{\# Function to extract mismatches:}
\NormalTok{unmatched\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  dfs, tracker,}
\NormalTok{  years\_of\_interest,}
\NormalTok{  methods, thresholds}
\NormalTok{  ) \{}
  \CommentTok{\# Compute two‐digit suffixes}
\NormalTok{  suffixes }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{substr}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.character}\NormalTok{(years\_of\_interest), }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Run merge\_dfs\_into\_tracker on each df, extract unmatched\_df, add source}
\NormalTok{  result\_list }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(dfs), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(nm) \{}
\NormalTok{    out }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{merge\_dfs\_into\_tracker}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{dfs =}\NormalTok{ dfs[nm], }\AttributeTok{tracker =}\NormalTok{ tracker,}
      \AttributeTok{years\_of\_interest =}\NormalTok{ years\_of\_interest,}
      \AttributeTok{methods =}\NormalTok{ methods, }\AttributeTok{thresholds =}\NormalTok{ thresholds}
\NormalTok{    )}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{unmatched[[nm]]}
    
    \CommentTok{\# Add source column of length nrow(out)}
\NormalTok{    out }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ out }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{source =}\NormalTok{ nm)}
\NormalTok{    out}
\NormalTok{  \})}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Bind their rows}
\NormalTok{  combined }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(result\_list)}
  
  \CommentTok{\# Coalesce the district\_/state\_ columns}
\NormalTok{  state\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ combined }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{starts\_with}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_"}\NormalTok{), }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{contains}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"code"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{()}
\NormalTok{  dist\_cols }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ combined }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{starts\_with}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"district\_"}\NormalTok{), }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{contains}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"code"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{()}
  
\NormalTok{  combined }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
      \AttributeTok{district =} \FunctionTok{do.call}\NormalTok{(coalesce, }\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(., }\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(dist\_cols))),}
      \AttributeTok{state =} \FunctionTok{do.call}\NormalTok{(coalesce, }\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(., }\FunctionTok{all\_of}\NormalTok{(state\_cols)))}
\NormalTok{    ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(district, state, source)}
\NormalTok{\}}





\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Compare outcomes with different tracker dfs \#\#\#\#}

\CommentTok{\# Identify errors for each tracker df}
\NormalTok{unmatched\_rows\_timeseries }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{unmatched\_rows}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{dfs =}\NormalTok{ dfs, }\AttributeTok{tracker =}\NormalTok{ district\_timeseries,}
  \AttributeTok{years\_of\_interest =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"2001"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"2011"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"2024"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{methods =}\NormalTok{ methods, }\AttributeTok{thresholds =}\NormalTok{ thresholds}
\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{unmatched\_rows\_tracker }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{unmatched\_rows}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{dfs =}\NormalTok{ dfs, }\AttributeTok{tracker =}\NormalTok{ district\_tracker,}
  \AttributeTok{years\_of\_interest =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"2001"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"2011"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"2024"}\NormalTok{),}
  \AttributeTok{methods =}\NormalTok{ methods, }\AttributeTok{thresholds =}\NormalTok{ thresholds}
\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{\# Combine all errors}
\NormalTok{unmatched\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{full\_join}\NormalTok{(unmatched\_rows\_timeseries, unmatched\_rows\_tracker, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{join\_by}\NormalTok{(state, district), }\AttributeTok{suffix =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_timeseries"}\NormalTok{,}\StringTok{"\_tracker"}\NormalTok{))}


\CommentTok{\# Create a df with all rows from original data, so I can search for close matches easily}

\NormalTok{all\_rows }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(}
  \FunctionTok{lapply}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{names}\NormalTok{(dfs), }\ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(nm) dfs[[nm]] }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{source =}\NormalTok{ nm)),}
\NormalTok{  missing\_districts\_1718 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{source =} \StringTok{"missing\_districts\_1718"}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{  missing\_districts\_0708 }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{source =} \StringTok{"missing\_districts\_0708"}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{  district\_timeseries }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{source =} \StringTok{"district\_timeseries"}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{  district\_tracker }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{source =} \StringTok{"district\_tracker"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{state =} \FunctionTok{coalesce}\NormalTok{(}
      \SpecialCharTok{!!!}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(., }\FunctionTok{starts\_with}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"state\_"}\NormalTok{), }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{contains}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"code"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{district =} \FunctionTok{coalesce}\NormalTok{(}
      \SpecialCharTok{!!!}\FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(., }\FunctionTok{starts\_with}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"district\_"}\NormalTok{), }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\FunctionTok{contains}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"code"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{    )}
\NormalTok{  ) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(state, district, source)}

\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Read the images}
\NormalTok{img1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_read}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"map\_EMIE.png"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{img2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_read}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"map\_consumption.png"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{img3 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_read}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"map\_pucca.png"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{img4 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_read}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"map\_edu.png"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Set a standard width, then pad all to a common size}
\NormalTok{target\_width }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1200}
\NormalTok{target\_height }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{900}

\CommentTok{\# Resize each image by width while preserving aspect ratio}
\NormalTok{img1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_resize}\NormalTok{(img1, }\AttributeTok{geometry =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(target\_width))}
\NormalTok{img2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_resize}\NormalTok{(img2, }\AttributeTok{geometry =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(target\_width))}
\NormalTok{img3 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_resize}\NormalTok{(img3, }\AttributeTok{geometry =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(target\_width))}
\NormalTok{img4 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_resize}\NormalTok{(img4, }\AttributeTok{geometry =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(target\_width))}

\CommentTok{\# \# Then pad with white (or transparent) space to ensure equal height \& width for alignment}
\CommentTok{\# img1 \textless{}{-} image\_extent(img1, paste0(target\_width, "x", target\_height), gravity = "center", color = "white")}
\CommentTok{\# img2 \textless{}{-} image\_extent(img2, paste0(target\_width, "x", target\_height), gravity = "center", color = "white")}
\CommentTok{\# img3 \textless{}{-} image\_extent(img3, paste0(target\_width, "x", target\_height), gravity = "center", color = "white")}
\CommentTok{\# img4 \textless{}{-} image\_extent(img4, paste0(target\_width, "x", target\_height), gravity = "center", color = "white")}

\CommentTok{\# \# Combine}
\NormalTok{top\_row }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_append}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(img1, img2))}
\NormalTok{bottom\_row }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_append}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(img3, img4))}
\NormalTok{collage }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_append}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(top\_row, bottom\_row), }\AttributeTok{stack =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{\#collage \textless{}{-} image\_append(c(img1, img2, img3, img4), stack = TRUE)}

\FunctionTok{image\_write}\NormalTok{(collage, }\AttributeTok{path =} \StringTok{"collage1\_map.png"}\NormalTok{)}



\CommentTok{\# Read the images}
\NormalTok{img5 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_read}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"map\_region.png"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{img6 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{image\_read}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"map\_ling\_dist.png"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# img6 \textless{}{-} image\_extent(img6, paste0(target\_width, "x", target\_height), gravity = "center", color = "white")}

\section*{Chunk 24: Geospatial: Neighbor list construction}\label{chunk-24-geospatial-neighbor-list-construction}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 24: Geospatial: Neighbor list construction}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{joined\_df }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ joined\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{drop\_na}\NormalTok{()}

\CommentTok{\# \# Test results under different contiguity measures; code based on @liChapter14Spatial2019}
\CommentTok{\# remotes::install\_github("spatialanalysis/sfExtras")}
\CommentTok{\# library(sfExtras)}
\CommentTok{\# rook\_neighbors \textless{}{-} joined\_geom \%\textgreater{}\% st\_rook()}
\CommentTok{\# rook\_neighbors \%\textgreater{}\% lengths() \%\textgreater{}\% mean()}
\CommentTok{\# \# 4.780165 average neighbors per district}
\CommentTok{\# queen\_neighbors \textless{}{-} joined\_geom \%\textgreater{}\% st\_queen()}
\CommentTok{\# queen\_neighbors \%\textgreater{}\% lengths() \%\textgreater{}\% mean()}
\CommentTok{\# \# 4.783471}
\CommentTok{\# \# Average neighbor counts are nearly equivalent}

\CommentTok{\# \# Test for fastest contiguity measure}
\CommentTok{\# start.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\NormalTok{nb\_2020 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ joined\_df }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}  
  \FunctionTok{poly2nb}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{queen =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{)}
\CommentTok{\# end.time \textless{}{-} Sys.time()}
\CommentTok{\# end.time {-} start.time}
\CommentTok{\# \# With queen = TRUE: 32.64976 secs}
\CommentTok{\# \# With queen = FALSE: 31.15051 secs}
\CommentTok{\# \# Rook contiguity slightly faster}

\CommentTok{\# Binary adjacency matrix. Rook{-}contiguity neighbor list used for speed, conceptual interpretability}
\NormalTok{W\_2020 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nb2mat}\NormalTok{(nb\_2020, }\AttributeTok{style =} \StringTok{"B"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{zero.policy =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }
\CommentTok{\# W\_2020[i,j] == 1 if districts i and j share a border, 0 else}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\NormalTok{    ),}
    \AttributeTok{.names =} \StringTok{"\{.col\}\_\{.fn\}"}
\NormalTok{  )) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{pivot\_longer}\NormalTok{(}

\section*{Chunk 28: Multicollinearity check}\label{chunk-28-multicollinearity-check}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{Chunk 28: Multicollinearity check}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{X }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"EMIE"}\NormalTok{, controls\_needlag, controls\_nolag) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{reformulate}\NormalTok{() }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{model.matrix}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ joined\_df)}

\CommentTok{\# \# Number of independent columns:}
\CommentTok{\# qr(X)$rank}
\CommentTok{\# \# Num. total columns:}
\CommentTok{\# ncol(X)}
\CommentTok{\# \# Recall: If qr(X)$rank \textless{} ncol(X), exact collinearity.}

\CommentTok{\# Heuristic: kappa\textgreater{}30 implies severe multicollinearity}
\NormalTok{X\_no\_intercept }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ X[, }\FunctionTok{colnames}\NormalTok{(X) }\SpecialCharTok{!=} \StringTok{"(Intercept)"}\NormalTok{, drop }\OtherTok{=} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{keep }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{apply}\NormalTok{(X\_no\_intercept, }\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, sd, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}} \DecValTok{0}
\NormalTok{X\_scaled }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{scale}\NormalTok{(X\_no\_intercept[, keep, }\AttributeTok{drop =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}\NormalTok{])}
\NormalTok{kappa\_val }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{kappa}\NormalTok{(X\_scaled, }\AttributeTok{exact =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# \# Check for linear dependence}
\CommentTok{\# X\_df \textless{}{-} as.data.frame(X\_scaled)}
\CommentTok{\# alias(lm(}
\CommentTok{\#   consumption\_pct\_change \textasciitilde{} .,}
\CommentTok{\#   data = cbind(consumption\_pct\_change = joined\_df$consumption\_pct\_change, X\_df)}
\CommentTok{\# ))}

\CommentTok{\# \# Heuristic: VIF \textgreater{} 10 implies problematic collinearity}
\CommentTok{\# vif(lm(}
\CommentTok{\#   reformulate(}
\CommentTok{\#     c("EMIE", controls\_needlag, controls\_nolag),}
\CommentTok{\#     response = "consumption\_pct\_change"}
\CommentTok{\#   ),}
\CommentTok{\#   data = joined\_df}
\CommentTok{\# ))}
\CommentTok{\# }
\CommentTok{\# vif(model\_consumption\_iv)}
\CommentTok{\# vif(model\_gini\_iv)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Build row‑standardized spatial weights (listw) object}
\CommentTok{\# Recall: Number+order of rows in 2SLS models = number+order used for spatial weights}
\NormalTok{listw\_2020 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nb2listw}\NormalTok{(nb\_2020, }\AttributeTok{style =} \StringTok{"W"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{zero.policy =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# TRUE for, say, islands}

\CommentTok{\# Global Moran’s I on residuals}

\CommentTok{\# \# p{-}vals via Monte Carlo (moran.test() assumes asymptotic normality)}
\CommentTok{\# set.seed(999)}
\CommentTok{\# num\_m = 9999}
\CommentTok{\# mc \textless{}{-} moran.mc(resid\_cons, listw\_2020, nsim = num\_m)}
\CommentTok{\# plot(mc)}
\CommentTok{\# mc$p.value}

\CommentTok{\# \# Before more controls were added in:}

\CommentTok{\# \# 2.779572e{-}23}
\CommentTok{\# m\_gini\_resid$p.value}
\CommentTok{\# \# 2.033012e{-}40}
\CommentTok{\# m\_fscons\_resid$p.value}
\CommentTok{\# \# 1.189148e{-}105}

\CommentTok{\# Moran’s I on explanatory variable and IV}
\NormalTok{m\_EMIE }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{moran.test}\NormalTok{(joined\_df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{EMIE, listw\_2020, }\AttributeTok{zero.policy =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{m\_wavg\_ling\_degrees }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{moran.test}\NormalTok{(joined\_df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{wavg\_ling\_degrees, listw\_2020, }\AttributeTok{zero.policy =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# m\_EMIE$p.value}
\CommentTok{\# \# 8.990354e{-}180}
\CommentTok{\# m\_wavg\_ling\_degrees$p.value}
\CommentTok{\# \# 1.721903e{-}254}
\CommentTok{\# All very extreme}

\CommentTok{\# Each of the following are named; put them in unname() to get the raw number}
\CommentTok{\# m\_EMIE$statistic = z{-}score}
\CommentTok{\# m\_EMIE$estimate[1] = Moran\textquotesingle{}s I statistic}
\CommentTok{\# m\_EMIE$estimate[2] = expected value of Moran\textquotesingle{}s I under the null (no spatial autocorrelation i.e., randomized locations)}
\CommentTok{\# m\_EMIE$estimate[3] = variance under the null}


\CommentTok{\# Test Moran’s I on the response variables}
\NormalTok{m\_cons }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{moran.test}\NormalTok{(joined\_df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{consumption\_pct\_change, listw\_2020, }\AttributeTok{zero.policy=}\ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# m\_cons$p.value}
\CommentTok{\# 1.608813e{-}26}
\CommentTok{\# m\_gini$p.value}
\CommentTok{\# 8.51626e{-}22}

\CommentTok{\# Repeat for controls which may have a strong degree of spatial autocorrelation (infrastructure, poverty, etc.)}

\DocumentationTok{\#\#\#\# Test instrument\textquotesingle{}s strength \#\#\#\#}

\CommentTok{\# Run cluster{-}robust Wald F{-}test}
\NormalTok{vcov\_partialf }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{vcovCL}\NormalTok{(first\_stage\_consumption, }\AttributeTok{cluster =}\NormalTok{ joined\_df}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{state\_20)}

\NormalTok{partial\_F\_test }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{linearHypothesis}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  first\_stage\_consumption,}
  \StringTok{"wavg\_ling\_degrees = 0"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{vcov. =}\NormalTok{ vcov\_partialf,}
  \AttributeTok{test =} \StringTok{"F"}
\NormalTok{) }\CommentTok{\# Wald F{-}stat with robust vcov + one endogenous regressor "is equivalent to the Kleibergen{-}Paap statistic" (https://lrberge.github.io/fixest/reference/fitstat.html)}

\CommentTok{\# Extract F{-}stat and p{-}val}
\NormalTok{partial\_f }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ partial\_F\_test[[}\StringTok{"F"}\NormalTok{]][}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{partial\_p }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ partial\_F\_test[[}\StringTok{"Pr(\textgreater{}F)"}\NormalTok{]][}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{]}

\CommentTok{\# Create asterisks based on p{-}val}
\NormalTok{stars }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \ControlFlowTok{function}\NormalTok{(p) \{}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (p }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.001}\NormalTok{) }\FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"***"}\NormalTok{)}
  \ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (p }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.01}\NormalTok{) }\FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"**"}\NormalTok{)}
  \ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{ (p }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{) }\FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"*"}\NormalTok{)}
  \ControlFlowTok{else} \FunctionTok{return}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{""}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}

\CommentTok{\# Add custom GOF row for the partial F{-}stat}
\NormalTok{custom\_gof\_row }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}
  \AttributeTok{term =} \StringTok{"Instrument\textquotesingle{}s F{-}Statistic"}\NormalTok{,}
  \AttributeTok{estimate =} \FunctionTok{paste0}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{formatC}\NormalTok{(partial\_f, }\AttributeTok{digits =} \DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{format =} \StringTok{"f"}\NormalTok{), }\FunctionTok{stars}\NormalTok{(partial\_p)),}
  \AttributeTok{stringsAsFactors =} \ConstantTok{FALSE}
\NormalTok{)}
